# Surah 14 — Ibrahim

**Status:** ✅ Publishable · Fidelity 100/100 · Prose overlap (4-gram) 0.068 · Longest prose run 16 words · Em dashes 0

## 14:1-3 — verses 1-3 (shared commentary)

### Translation

Tafsir of Surat Ibrahim (peace be upon him)

It is Meccan.

In the name of Allah, the Most Gracious, the Most Merciful.

The discussion of the disjointed letters at the openings of the surahs has already preceded.

{A Book which We have sent down to you} meaning: this is a Book which We have sent down to you, O Muhammad ﷺ, and it is the Magnificent Qur'an, which is the noblest Book that Allah sent down from heaven, upon the noblest Messenger whom Allah sent forth on earth, to all its people, its Arabs and its non-Arabs.

{that you may bring mankind out of the darknesses into the light} meaning: We sent you, O Muhammad ﷺ, with this Book only that you might bring mankind out of the misguidance and error in which they were, into guidance and right conduct, as He said: {Allah is the ally of those who believe; He brings them out of the darknesses into the light. And those who disbelieve, their allies are false gods; they bring them out of the light into the darknesses} [al-Baqarah: 257], and He, Exalted is He, said: {It is He who sends down upon His servant clear signs that He may bring you out of the darknesses into the light} [al-Hadid: 9].

Regarding His saying: {by the permission of their Lord}, meaning: He is the One who guides whomever He has decreed guidance for, at the hands of His Messenger sent forth by His command, guiding them {to the path of the Mighty}, that is, the Mighty One who cannot be resisted or overcome, rather He is the Subduer of all besides Him, "the Praiseworthy," meaning: praised in all His deeds and words, in His legislation, His command and His prohibition, truthful in His report.

Regarding His saying: {Allah, to whom belongs whatever is in the heavens and whatever is on the earth}, some read it as a new sentence in the nominative case, while others read it in agreement, as a description of the Majestic Name, as He, Exalted is He, said: {Say: O mankind, indeed I am the Messenger of Allah to you all, He to whom belongs the dominion of the heavens and the earth} [al-A'raf: 158].

Regarding His saying: {and woe to the disbelievers from a severe punishment}, meaning: woe be to them on the Day of Resurrection, since they opposed you, O Muhammad ﷺ, and denied you.

Then He described them as loving the life of this world more than the Hereafter, that is, they give it precedence and prefer it over the Hereafter, and they work for this world and forget the Hereafter, casting it behind their backs, {and hinder from the path of Allah}, which is the following of the messengers, {and seek to make it crooked}, meaning: they love that the path of Allah be crooked, deviating and swerving, whereas it is in itself straight, unharmed by whoever opposes it or forsakes it. So they, in seeking that, are in ignorance and misguidance far removed from the truth, and no good outcome can be hoped for them, given this state of theirs.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

تَفْسِيرُ سُورَةِ إِبْرَاهِيمَ عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ

وَهِيَ مَكِّيَّةٌ.

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَنِ الرَّحِيمِ

* *

قَدْ تَقَدَّمَ الْكَلَامُ عَلَى الْحُرُوفِ الْمُقَطَّعَةِ فِي أَوَائِلِ السُّورِ.

﴿كِتَابٌ أَنزلْنَاهُ إِلَيْكَ﴾ أَيْ: هَذَا كِتَابٌ أَنْزَلْنَاهُ إِلَيْكَ يَا مُحَمَّدُ، وَهُوَ الْقُرْآنُ الْعَظِيمُ، الَّذِي هُوَ أَشْرَفُ كِتَابٍ أَنْزَلَهُ اللَّهُ مِنَ السَّمَاءِ، عَلَى أَشْرَفِ رَسُولٍ بَعَثَهُ اللَّهُ فِي الْأَرْضِ، إِلَى جَمِيعِ أَهْلِهَا عَرِبِهِمْ وَعَجَمِهِمْ .

﴿لِتُخْرِجَ النَّاسَ مِنَ الظُّلُمَاتِ إِلَى النُّورِ﴾ أَيْ: إِنَّمَا بَعَثْنَاكَ يَا مُحَمَّدُ بِهَذَا الْكِتَابِ؛ لِتُخْرِجَ النَّاسَ مِمَّا هُمْ فِيهِ مِنَ الضَّلَالِ وَالْغَيِّ إِلَى الْهُدَى وَالرُّشْدِ، كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿اللَّهُ وَلِيُّ الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا يُخْرِجُهُمْ مِنَ الظُّلُمَاتِ إِلَى النُّورِ وَالَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا أَوْلِيَاؤُهُمُ الطَّاغُوتُ يُخْرِجُونَهُمْ مِنَ النُّورِ إِلَى الظُّلُمَاتِ﴾ الْآيَةَ [الْبَقَرَةِ: ٢٥٧] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿هُوَ الَّذِي يُنزلُ عَلَى عَبْدِهِ آيَاتٍ بَيِّنَاتٍ لِيُخْرِجَكُمْ مِنَ الظُّلُمَاتِ إِلَى النُّورِ﴾ [الْحَدِيدِ: ٩] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿بِإِذْنِ رَبِّهِمْ﴾ أَيْ: هُوَ الْهَادِي لِمَنْ قَدر لَهُ الْهِدَايَةَ عَلَى يَدَيْ رَسُولِهِ الْمَبْعُوثِ عَنْ أَمْرِهِ يُهْدِيهِمْ ﴿إِلَى صِرَاطِ الْعَزِيزِ﴾ أَيِ: الْعَزِيزِ الَّذِي لَا يُمَانَعُ وَلَا يُغَالَبُ، بَلْ هُوَ الْقَاهِرُ لِكُلِّ مَا سِوَاهُ، "الْحَمِيدُ" أَيِ: الْمَحْمُودُ فِي جَمِيعِ أَفْعَالِهِ وَأَقْوَالِهِ، وَشَرْعِهِ وَأَمْرِهِ وَنَهْيِهِ، الصَّادِقُ فِي خَبَرِهِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿اللَّهِ الَّذِي لَهُ مَا فِي السَّمَاوَاتِ وَمَا فِي الأرْضِ﴾ قَرَأَهُ بَعْضُهُمْ مُسْتَأْنَفًا مَرْفُوعًا، وَقَرَأَهُ آخَرُونَ عَلَى الْإِتْبَاعِ صِفَةً لِلْجَلَالَةِ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿قُلْ يَا أَيُّهَا النَّاسُ إِنِّي رَسُولُ اللَّهِ إِلَيْكُمْ جَمِيعًا الَّذِي لَهُ مُلْكُ السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالأرْضِ﴾ [الْأَعْرَافِ: ١٥٨] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَوَيْلٌ لِلْكَافِرِينَ مِنْ عَذَابٍ شَدِيدٍ﴾ أَيْ: وَيْلٌ لَهُمْ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ إِذْ خَالَفُوكَ يَا مُحَمَّدُ وَكَذَّبُوكَ.

ثُمَّ وَصَفَهُمْ بِأَنَّهُمْ يَسْتَحِبُّونَ الْحَيَاةَ الدُّنْيَا عَلَى الْآخِرَةِ، أَيْ: يُقَدِّمُونَهَا ويُؤثرونها عَلَيْهَا، وَيَعْمَلُونَ لِلدُّنْيَا ونَسُوا الْآخِرَةَ، وَتَرَكُوهَا وَرَاءَ ظُهُورِهِمْ، ﴿وَيَصُدُّونَ عَنْ سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ﴾ وَهِيَ اتِّبَاعُ الرُّسُلِ ﴿وَيَبْغُونَهَا عِوَجًا﴾ أَيْ: وَيُحِبُّونَ أَنْ تَكُونَ سَبِيلُ اللَّهِ عِوَجًا مَائِلَةً عَائِلَةً وَهِيَ مُسْتَقِيمَةٌ فِي نَفْسِهَا، لَا يَضُرُّهَا مَنْ خَالَفَهَا وَلَا مَنْ خَذَلَهَا، فَهُمْ فِي ابْتِغَائِهِمْ ذَلِكَ فِي جَهْلٍ وَضَلَالٍ بَعِيدٍ مِنَ الْحَقِّ، لَا يُرْجَى لَهُمْ -وَالْحَالَةُ هَذِهِ -صَلَاحٌ.

---

## 14:4 — verse 4

### Translation

This is part of His gentleness, exalted is He, toward His creation: that He sends to them messengers from among themselves, speaking their languages, so that they may understand from them what they want to convey and what they were sent to them with, as Imam Ahmad said:

[chain] Waki', from 'Umar ibn Dharr, who said: Mujahid said, from Abu Dharr, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said, "Allah, mighty and exalted, never sent a prophet except in the language of his people."

His saying: {So Allah leads astray whom He wills and guides whom He wills} means: after the clarification and the establishment of the proof against them, He, exalted is He, leads astray whom He wills from the path of guidance, and guides whom He wills to the truth. {And He is the Almighty}, the One whose will is always realized and whose will not to do a thing means it never happens, {the Wise} in His actions, leading astray whoever deserves to be led astray, and guiding whoever is worthy of guidance.

This was Allah's established way among His creation: He never sent a prophet to a nation except in their own language. Thus each prophet was singled out to convey his message to his own nation and no others, while Muhammad ibn 'Abdullah, the Messenger of Allah, was singled out with a message general to all people, as is established in the two Sahihs from Jabir, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said, "I have been given five things that no prophet before me was given: I was aided with terror that reaches a month's journey away, the earth was made for me a place of prayer and a means of purification, the spoils of war were made lawful for me, and were not made lawful for anyone before me, I was given intercession, and every prophet before was sent to his own people, while I have been sent to all mankind."

This has corroborating reports from many angles. And Allah, exalted is He, said: {Say, O mankind, indeed I am the Messenger of Allah to you all} [al-A'raf: 158].

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

هَذَا مِنْ لُطْفِهِ تَعَالَى بِخَلْقِهِ: أَنَّهُ يُرْسِلُ إِلَيْهِمْ رُسُلًا مِنْهُمْ بِلُغَاتِهِمْ لِيَفْهَمُوا عَنْهُمْ مَا يُرِيدُونَ وَمَا أُرْسِلُوا بِهِ إِلَيْهِمْ، كَمَا قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ:

حَدَّثَنَا وَكِيعٌ، عَنْ عُمَرَ بْنِ ذَرٍ قَالَ: قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: عَنْ أَبِي ذَرٍّ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "لَمْ يَبْعَثِ اللَّهُ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، نَبِيًّا إِلَّا بِلُغَةِ قَوْمِهِ" .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَيُضِلُّ اللَّهُ مَنْ يَشَاءُ وَيَهْدِي مَنْ يَشَاءُ﴾ أَيْ: بَعْدَ الْبَيَانِ وَإِقَامَةِ الْحُجَّةِ عَلَيْهِمْ يَضِلُّ تَعَالَى مَنْ يَشَاءُ عَنْ وَجْهِ الْهُدَى، وَيَهْدِي مَنْ يَشَاءُ إِلَى الْحَقِّ، ﴿وَهُوَ الْعَزِيزُ﴾ الَّذِي مَا شَاءَ كَانَ، وَمَا لَمْ يَشَأْ لَمْ يَكُنْ، ﴿الْحَكِيمُ﴾ فِي أَفْعَالِهِ، فَيُضِلُّ مَنْ يَسْتَحِقُّ الْإِضْلَالَ، وَيَهْدِي مَنْ هُوَ أَهْلٌ لِذَلِكَ.

وَقَدْ كَانَتْ هَذِهِ سُنَّةُ اللَّهِ فِي خَلْقِهِ: أَنَّهُ مَا بَعَثَ نَبِيًّا فِي أُمَّةٍ إِلَّا أَنْ يَكُونَ بِلُغَتِهِمْ، فَاخْتَصَّ كُلَّ نَبِيٍّ بِإِبْلَاغِ رِسَالَتِهِ إِلَى أُمَّتِهِ دُونَ غَيْرِهِمْ، وَاخْتَصَّ مُحَمَّدَ بْنَ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ بِعُمُومِ الرِّسَالَةِ إِلَى سَائِرِ النَّاسِ، كَمَا ثَبَتَ فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ عَنْ جَابِرٍ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "أُعْطِيتُ خَمْسًا لَمْ يُعطَهُن أَحَدٌ مِنَ الْأَنْبِيَاءِ قَبْلِي: نُصِرْتُ بِالرُّعْبِ مَسِيرَةَ شَهْرٍ، وَجُعِلَتْ لِي الْأَرْضُ مَسْجِدًا وطَهُورًا، وأحلَّت لِيَ الْغَنَائِمُ وَلَمْ تُحَلَّ لِأَحَدٍ قَبْلِي، وَأُعْطِيتُ الشَّفَاعَةَ، وَكَانَ النَّبِيُّ يُبْعَثُ إِلَى قَوْمِهِ، وَبُعِثْتُ إِلَى النَّاسِ عَامَّةً" .

وَلَهُ شَوَاهِدُ مِنْ وُجُوهٍ كَثِيرَةٍ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿قُلْ يَا أَيُّهَا النَّاسُ إِنِّي رَسُولُ اللَّهِ إِلَيْكُمْ جَمِيعًا﴾ [الأعراف: ١٥٨] .

---

## 14:5 — verse 5

### Translation

The Exalted says: Just as We sent you, O Muhammad, and revealed to you the Book, so that you might bring all people out, calling them to come out of the darknesses into the light, likewise We sent Musa among the Children of Israel with Our signs.

Mujahid said: these are the nine signs.

{That: Bring your people out of the darknesses} means: We commanded him, saying to him: {Bring your people out of the darknesses into the light}, that is, call them to good, so that they might come out of the darknesses of the ignorance and misguidance they were in, into the light of guidance and the insight of faith.

{And remind them of the days of Allah} means: of His bounties and favors upon them, in bringing them out of the bondage of Pharaoh,

and his tyranny, injustice, and oppression, and His delivering them from their enemy, His splitting the sea for them, His shading them with clouds, His sending down manna and quails upon them, and other favors besides these. This was said by Mujahid, Qatadah, and more than one other.

There has come regarding this the elevated hadith which Abdullah ibn al-Imam Ahmad ibn Hanbal narrated in the Musnad of his father, where he said: [chain] Yahya ibn Abdullah, freedman of the Banu Hashim, narrated to me, Muhammad ibn Aban al-Ju'fi narrated to us, from Abu Ishaq, from Sa'id ibn Jubayr [from Ibn Abbas, from Ubayy ibn Ka'b, from the Prophet ﷺ concerning the saying of the Blessed and Exalted, {And remind them of the days of Allah}, he said: "the bounties of Allah, Blessed and Exalted."]

[Ibn Jarir narrated it] and Ibn Abi Hatim, from the hadith of Muhammad ibn Aban, through him. Abdullah his son also narrated it as mawquf (halted report), and that is more fitting.

His saying: {Indeed in that are signs for every steadfast, grateful one} means: indeed in what We did with Our close ones, the Children of Israel, when We rescued them from the hand of Pharaoh and delivered them from the degrading punishment they were in, there is a lesson for every steadfast one, that is, in adversity, and grateful one, that is, in ease, just as Qatadah said: What an excellent servant is a servant who, when tried, is steadfast, and when given, is grateful.

And likewise it has come in the authentic hadith from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ that he said: "Indeed the affair of the believer is altogether wondrous. Allah does not decree anything for him except that it is good for him. If adversity befalls him, he is steadfast, and that is good for him, and if ease befalls him, he is grateful, and that is good for him."

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: وَكَمَا أَرْسَلْنَاكَ يَا مُحَمَّدُ وأَنْزَلْنَا عَلَيْكَ الْكِتَابَ، لِتُخْرِجَ النَّاسَ كُلَّهُمْ، تَدْعُوهُمْ إِلَى الْخُرُوجِ مِنَ الظُّلُمَاتِ إِلَى النُّورِ، كَذَلِكَ أَرْسَلْنَا مُوسَى فِي بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ بِآيَاتِنَا.

قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: وَهِيَ التِّسْعُ الْآيَاتِ.

﴿أَنْ أَخْرِجْ قَوْمَكَ مِنَ الظُّلُمَاتِ﴾ أَيْ: أَمَرْنَاهُ قَائِلِينَ لَهُ: ﴿أَخْرِجْ قَوْمَكَ مِنَ الظُّلُمَاتِ إِلَى النُّورِ﴾ أَيِ: ادْعُهُمْ إِلَى الْخَيْرِ، لِيَخْرُجُوا مِنْ ظُلُمَاتِ مَا كَانُوا فِيهِ مِنَ الْجَهْلِ وَالضَّلَالِ إِلَى نُورِ الْهُدَى وَبَصِيرَةِ الْإِيمَانِ.

﴿وَذَكِّرْهُمْ بِأَيَّامِ اللَّهِ﴾ أَيْ: بِأَيَادِيهِ ونعَمه عَلَيْهِمْ، فِي إِخْرَاجِهِ إِيَّاهُمْ مِنْ أَسْرِ فِرْعَوْنَ.

وَقَهْرِهِ وَظُلْمِهِ وَغَشْمِهِ، وَإِنْجَائِهِ إِيَّاهُمْ مِنْ عَدْوِهِمْ، وَفَلْقِهِ لَهُمُ الْبَحْرَ، وَتَظْلِيلِهِ إِيَّاهُمْ بِالْغَمَامِ، وَإِنْزَالِهِ عَلَيْهِمُ الْمَنَّ وَالسَّلْوَى، إِلَى غَيْرِ ذَلِكَ مِنَ النِّعَمِ. قَالَ ذَلِكَ مُجَاهِدٌ، وَقَتَادَةُ، وَغَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ.

وَقَدْ وَرَدَ فِيهِ الْحَدِيثُ الْمَرْفُوعُ الَّذِي رَوَاهُ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ الْإِمَامِ أَحْمَدَ بْنِ حَنْبَلٍ فِي مُسْنَدِ أَبِيهِ حَيْثُ قَالَ: حَدَّثَنِي يَحْيَى بْنُ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ مَوْلَى بَنِي هَاشِمٍ، حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ أَبَانٍ الْجُعْفِيُّ، عَنْ أَبِي إِسْحَاقَ، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْرٍ [عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، عَنْ أُبَيِّ بْنِ كَعْبٍ، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ فِي قَوْلِهِ تَبَارَكَ وَتَعَالَى: ﴿وَذَكِّرْهُمْ بِأَيَّامِ اللَّهِ﴾ قَالَ: "بِنِعَمِ اللَّهِ تَبَارَكَ وَتَعَالَى] " .

[وَرَوَاهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ] وَابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ أَبَانٍ، بِهِ وَرَوَاهُ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ ابْنُهُ أَيْضًا مَوْقُوفًا وَهُوَ أَشْبَهُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿إِنَّ فِي ذَلِكَ لآيَاتٍ لِكُلِّ صَبَّارٍ شَكُورٍ﴾ أَيْ: إِنَّ فِيمَا صَنَعْنَا بِأَوْلِيَائِنَا بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ حِينَ أَنْقَذْنَاهُمْ مِنْ يَدِ فِرْعَوْنَ، وَأَنْجَيْنَاهُمْ مِمَّا كَانُوا فِيهِ مِنَ الْعَذَابِ الْمُهِينِ، لَعِبْرَةٌ لِكُلِّ صَبَّار، أَيْ: فِي الضَّرَّاءِ، شَكُورٌ، أَيْ: فِي السَّرَّاءِ، كَمَا قَالَ قَتَادَةُ: نِعْمَ الْعَبْدُ، عَبْدٌ إِذَا ابتُلِي صَبَر، وَإِذَا أُعْطِيَ شَكَرَ.

وَكَذَا جَاءَ فِي الصَّحِيحِ عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: "إِنَّ أَمْرَ الْمُؤْمِنِ كُلَّه عَجَب، لَا يَقْضِي اللَّهُ لَهُ قَضَاءً إِلَّا كَانَ خَيْرًا لَهُ، إِنْ أَصَابَتْهُ ضَرَّاءُ صَبَرَ فَكَانَ خَيْرًا لَهُ، وَإِنْ أَصَابَتْهُ سَرَّاءُ شَكر فَكَانَ خيرا له" .

---

## 14:6-8 — verses 6-8 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says, informing us about Musa (peace be upon him), when he reminded his people of the days of Allah that they had experienced and His favors upon them, when He saved them from the house of Pharaoh and from the torment and humiliation those people used to inflict on them, when they used to slaughter whatever male children were found among them and leave their females alive. Allah rescued the Children of Israel from that, and this is a tremendous favor. That is why He said: {And in that was a great trial from your Lord}, meaning: a great favor from Him upon you in that, one which you are incapable of properly thanking Him for.

It has also been said: and in what the people of Pharaoh used to do to you of those deeds, {a trial}, meaning a great test. It is possible that both meanings are intended, and Allah knows best, just as He said: {And We tested them with good things and bad, that they might return} [al-A'raf: 168].

His saying {And when your Lord proclaimed} means: He informed you and made known to you His promise to you. It is also possible that the meaning is: when your Lord swore an oath, swearing by His might, His majesty, and His greatness, as He said: {And when your Lord proclaimed that He would surely send upon them until the Day of Resurrection [those who would afflict them with the worst torment]} [al-A'raf: 167].

His saying {If you are grateful, I will surely increase you} means: if you are grateful for My favor upon you, I will surely increase you from it. {But if you are ungrateful} means: if you disbelieve in the favors, conceal them, and deny them, {then indeed My punishment is severe}, and that is by stripping the favors away from them and punishing them for their ingratitude toward them.

It has come in the hadith: "Indeed the servant is deprived of provision because of a sin he commits."

And in al-Musnad: that a beggar passed by the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, and he gave him a date, but the man became angry and refused to accept it. Then another beggar passed by, and he gave it to him, and he accepted it, saying: "A date from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ!" So the Prophet ordered forty dirhams to be given to him, or something like that.

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Aswad told us, Umara al-Saydalani told us, from Thabit, from Anas, who said: A beggar came to the Prophet ﷺ, and he ordered a date be given to him, but he did not take it, or he showed disdain for it. He said: then another one came to him, and he ordered a date be given to him, and he said: "Glory be to Allah! A date from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ!" So the Prophet said to the servant girl: "Go to Umm Salamah and give him the forty dirhams that are with her."

Imam Ahmad alone narrated this.

Umara ibn Zadhan was deemed reliable by Ibn Hibban, Ahmad, and Ya'qub ibn Sufyan. Ibn Ma'in said: "sound (salih)." Abu Zur'ah said: "there is no harm in him." Abu Hatim said: "his hadith is recorded but not relied upon as proof, he is not strong." Al-Bukhari said: "his hadith is sometimes confused." It is also reported from Ahmad that he said: "unrecognized (munkar) hadiths have been narrated from him." Abu Dawud said: "he is not that reliable." Al-Daraqutni weakened him, while Ibn Adi said: "there is no harm in him among those whose hadith is recorded."

The Almighty's saying: {And Musa said: If you disbelieve, you and everyone on earth altogether, then indeed Allah is Self-Sufficient (Ghani), Praiseworthy (Hamid)} means: He is free of need of the gratitude of His servants, and He is al-Hamid, the Praised One, and the disbelief of whoever disbelieves does not affect Him at all, just as He said: {If you disbelieve, then indeed Allah has no need of you. And He does not approve of disbelief for His servants. But if you are grateful, He approves it for you} [al-Zumar: 7]. And the Almighty said: {But they disbelieved and turned away, and Allah was not in need of them, and Allah is Self-Sufficient, Praiseworthy} [al-Taghabun: 6].

In Sahih Muslim, from Abu Dharr, from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, in what he related from his Lord, Mighty and Majestic, that He said: "O My servants, if the first of you and the last of you, your humans and your jinn, were all as pious as the most pious heart among you, that would not add anything to My dominion. O My servants, if the first of you and the last of you, your humans and your jinn, were all as wicked as the most wicked heart among you, that would not diminish anything from My dominion. O My servants, if the first of you and the last of you, your humans and your jinn, were to stand together in one place and ask of Me, and I gave every person what he asked for, that would not diminish My dominion at all, except as much as a needle diminishes the sea when it is dipped into it." Glorified and exalted is He, al-Ghani, al-Hamid.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُخْبِرًا عَنْ مُوسَى، حِينَ ذَكَّر قَوْمَهُ بِأَيَّامِ اللَّهِ عِنْدَهُمْ وَنِعَمَهُ عَلَيْهِمْ، إِذْ أَنْجَاهُمْ مِنْ آلِ فِرْعَوْنَ، وَمَا كَانُوا يَسُومُونَهُمْ بِهِ مِنَ الْعَذَابِ وَالْإِذْلَالِ، حِينَ كَانُوا يَذْبَحُونَ مَنْ وُجِدَ مِنْ أَبْنَائِهِمْ، وَيَتْرُكُونَ إِنَاثَهُمْ فَأَنْقَذَ اللَّهُ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ مِنْ ذَلِكَ، وَهَذِهِ نِعْمَةٌ عَظِيمَةٌ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿وَفِي ذَلِكُمْ بَلاءٌ مِنْ رَبِّكُمْ عَظِيمٌ﴾ أَيْ: نِعْمَةٌ عَظِيمَةٌ مِنْهُ عَلَيْكُمْ فِي ذَلِكَ، أَنْتُمْ عَاجِزُونَ عَنِ الْقِيَامِ بِشُكْرِهَا.

وَقِيلَ: وَفِيمَا كَانَ يَصْنَعُهُ بِكُمْ قَوْمُ فِرْعَوْنَ مِنْ تِلْكَ الْأَفَاعِيلِ ﴿بَلَاءٌ﴾ أَيِ: اخْتِبَارٌ عَظِيمٌ. وَيُحْتَمَلُ أَنْ يَكُونَ الْمُرَادُ هَذَا وَهَذَا، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَبَلَوْنَاهُمْ بِالْحَسَنَاتِ وَالسَّيِّئَاتِ لَعَلَّهُمْ يَرْجِعُونَ﴾ [الْأَعْرَافِ: ١٦٨] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَإِذْ تَأَذَّنَ رَبُّكُمْ﴾ أَيْ: آذَنَكُمْ وَأَعْلَمَكُمْ بِوَعْدِهِ لَكُمْ. وَيُحْتَمَلُ أَنْ يَكُونَ الْمَعْنَى: وَإِذْ أَقْسَمَ رَبُّكُمْ وَآلَى بِعِزَّتِهِ وَجَلَالِهِ وَكِبْرِيَائِهِ كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿وَإِذْ تَأَذَّنَ رَبُّكَ لَيَبْعَثَنَّ عَلَيْهِمْ إِلَى يَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ [مَنْ يَسُومُهُمْ سُوءَ الْعَذَابِ] ﴾ [الْأَعْرَافِ: ١٦٧] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ ﴿لَئِنْ شَكَرْتُمْ لأزِيدَنَّكُمْ﴾ أَيْ: لَئِنْ شَكَرْتُمْ نِعْمَتِي عَلَيْكُمْ لِأَزِيدَنَّكُمْ مِنْهَا، ﴿وَلَئِنْ كَفَرْتُمْ﴾ أَيْ: كَفَرْتُمُ النِّعَمَ وَسَتَرْتُمُوهَا وَجَحَدْتُمُوهَا، ﴿إِنَّ عَذَابِي لَشَدِيدٌ﴾ وَذَلِكَ بِسَلْبِهَا عَنْهُمْ، وَعِقَابِهِ إِيَّاهُمْ عَلَى كُفْرِهَا.

وَقَدْ جَاءَ فِي الْحَدِيثِ: "إِنَّ الْعَبْدَ لَيُحْرَمُ الرِّزْقَ بِالذَّنْبِ يُصِيبُهُ" .

وَفِي الْمُسْنَدِ: أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ مَرَّ بِهِ سَائِلٌ فَأَعْطَاهُ تَمْرَةً، فَتَسَخَّطها وَلَمْ يَقْبَلْهَا، ثُمَّ مَرَّ بِهِ آخَرُ فَأَعْطَاهُ إِيَّاهَا، فَقَبِلَهَا وَقَالَ: تَمْرَةٌ مِنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ، فَأَمَرَ لَهُ بِأَرْبَعِينَ دِرْهَمًا، أَوْ كَمَا قَالَ.

قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا أَسْودُ، حَدَّثَنَا عُمَارَةُ الصَّيدلاني، عَنْ ثَابِتٍ، عَنْ أَنَسٍ قَالَ: أَتَى النَّبِيَّ ﷺ سَائِلٌ فَأَمَرَ لَهُ بِتَمْرَةٍ فَلَمْ يَأْخُذْهَا -أَوْ: وَحِشَّ بِهَا -قَالَ: وَأَتَاهُ آخَرُ فَأَمَرَ لَهُ بِتَمْرَةٍ، فَقَالَ: سُبْحَانَ اللَّهِ! تَمْرَةٌ مِنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ. فَقَالَ لِلْجَارِيَةِ: "اذْهَبِي إِلَى أُمِّ سَلَمَةَ، فأعطيه الأربعين درهما التي عِنْدَهَا".

تَفَرَّدَ بِهِ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ .

وَعُمَارَةُ بْنُ زَاذَانَ وَثَّقَهُ ابْنُ حبَّان، وَأَحْمَدُ، وَيَعْقُوبُ بْنُ سُفْيَانَ وَقَالَ ابْنُ مَعِينٍ: صَالِحٌ. وَقَالَ أَبُو زُرْعَة: لَا بَأْسَ بِهِ. وَقَالَ أَبُو حَاتِمٍ: يكتب حديثه وَلَا يُحْتَجُّ بِهِ، لَيْسَ بِالْمَتِينِ. وَقَالَ الْبُخَارِيُّ: رُبَّمَا يُضْطَرَبُ فِي حَدِيثِهِ. وَعَنْ أَحْمَدَ أَيْضًا أَنَّهُ قَالَ: رُوِيَ عَنْهُ أَحَادِيثُ مُنْكِرَةٌ. وَقَالَ أَبُو دَاوُدَ: لَيْسَ بِذَاكَ. وَضَعَّفَهُ الدَّارَقُطْنِيُّ، وَقَالَ ابْنُ عَدِيٍّ: لَا بَأْسَ بِهِ مِمَّنْ يَكْتُبُ حَدِيثَهُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَقَالَ مُوسَى إِنْ تَكْفُرُوا أَنْتُمْ وَمَنْ فِي الأرْضِ جَمِيعًا فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ لَغَنِيٌّ حَمِيدٌ﴾ أَيْ: هُوَ غَنِيٌّ عَنْ شُكْرِ عِبَادِهِ، وَهُوَ الْحَمِيدُ الْمَحْمُودُ، وَإِنَّ كَفَرَهُ مَنْ كَفَرَهُ، كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿إِنْ تَكْفُرُوا فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ غَنِيٌّ عَنْكُمْ وَلا يَرْضَى لِعِبَادِهِ الْكُفْرَ وَإِنْ تَشْكُرُوا يَرْضَهُ لَكُمْ﴾ [الزُّمَرِ: ٧] وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿فَكَفَرُوا وَتَوَلَّوْا وَاسْتَغْنَى اللَّهُ وَاللَّهُ غَنِيٌّ حَمِيدٌ﴾ [التَّغَابُنِ: ٦] .

وَفِي صَحِيحِ مُسْلِمٍ، عَنْ أَبِي ذَرٍ، عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ فيما يَرْوِيهِ عَنْ رَبِّهِ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، أَنَّهُ قَالَ: "يَا عِبَادِي، لَوْ أَنَّ أَوَّلَكُمْ وَآخِرَكُمْ، وَإِنْسَكُمْ وَجِنَّكُمْ، كَانُوا عَلَى أَتْقَى قَلْبِ رَجُلٍ مِنْكُمْ، مَا زَادَ ذَلِكَ فِي مُلْكِي شَيْئًا. يَا عِبَادِي، لَوْ أَنَّ أَوَّلَكُمْ وَآخِرَكُمْ، وَإِنْسَكُمْ وَجِنَّكُمْ، كَانُوا عَلَى أَفْجَرِ قَلْبِ رَجُلٍ مِنْكُمْ، مَا نَقَصَ ذَلِكَ فِي مُلْكِي شَيْئًا. يَا عِبَادِي، لَوْ أن أولكم وآخركم، وإنسكم وجنكم، قاموا فِي صَعِيدٍ وَاحِدٍ، فَسَأَلُونِي، فَأَعْطَيْتُ كُلَّ إِنْسَانٍ مَسْأَلَتَهُ، مَا نَقَصَ ذَلِكَ مِنْ مُلْكِي شَيْئًا، إلا كما ينقُص المخْيَط إذا أدخل في الْبَحْرِ". فَسُبْحَانَهُ وَتَعَالَى الْغَنِيُّ الْحَمِيدُ .

---

## 14:9 — verse 9

### Translation

Ibn Jarir said: this is part of the completion of Moses' speech to his people.

Meaning: and his reminding them of the days of Allah, of His vengeance upon the nations that denied the messengers.

But there is a difficulty in what Ibn Jarir said. The apparent meaning is that this is a fresh report from Allah, Exalted is He, addressed to this nation (the Muslim community), for it has been said that the story of 'Ad and Thamud is not found in the Torah. If this had been part of Moses' speech to his people, in which he related this to them, there would be no doubt that these two stories would be found in the Torah. And Allah knows best. In sum, Allah, Exalted is He, has related to us the account of the people of Noah, 'Ad, Thamud, and other nations that denied the messengers, whose number none can count except Allah, Mighty and Majestic. Their messengers came to them with al-bayyinat (clear proofs), that is, with clear, dazzling, decisive arguments and evidences.

Ibn Ishaq said, from Amr ibn Maymun, from Abdullah, that he said concerning His statement: {None knows them except Allah}: the genealogists have lied.

Urwah ibn al-Zubayr said: we have not found anyone who knows what comes after Ma'add ibn Adnan.

Regarding His statement: {so they put their hands back into their mouths}, the exegetes differed as to its meaning. It was said: its meaning is that they gestured toward the mouths of the messengers, ordering them to be silent, when the messengers called them to Allah, Mighty and Majestic.

It was also said: rather, they placed their hands over their own mouths in denial of them.

It was also said: rather, it is an expression for their silence in response to the messengers.

Mujahid, Muhammad ibn Ka'b, and Qatadah said: its meaning is that they denied them and threw their words back at them with their own mouths.

Ibn Jarir said: the explanation of this is that "fi" (in) here carries the meaning of "bi" (with/by). He said: it has been heard from the Arabs, "Adkhalaka Allahu bi-l-jannah" (may Allah admit you by/with the Garden), meaning "into the Garden." And the poet said:

"And I desire it over Laqit and his kinsfolk... over Sinbis I do not desire..."

meaning: "I desire it with it (bi-ha)."

I (Ibn Kathir) say: what supports Mujahid's statement is the interpretation of that through the completion of the speech: {and they said, "Indeed we disbelieve in what you have been sent with, and indeed we are in disquieting doubt about that to which you call us"}. It is as though this, and Allah knows best, is an explanation of the meaning of their putting their hands back into their mouths.

Sufyan al-Thawri and Isra'il said, from Abu Ishaq, from Abu al-Ahwas, from Abdullah, concerning His statement: {so they put their hands back into their mouths}, he said: they bit them out of rage.

Shu'bah said, from Abu Ishaq, Abu Hubayrah ibn Maryam, from Abdullah, that he said the same. Abd al-Rahman ibn Zayd ibn Aslam chose this view, and Ibn Jarir explained it, favoring it, by citing His statement, Exalted is He, concerning the hypocrites: {and when they are alone, they bite their fingertips at you out of rage} [Al Imran: 119].

Al-Awfi said, from Ibn Abbas: when they heard the Book of Allah, they were amazed, and they brought their hands back to their mouths.

And they said: {Indeed we disbelieve in what you have been sent with, and indeed we are in disquieting doubt about that to which you call us}, meaning: we do not believe you in what you have brought, for we have strong doubt about it.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

قَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: هَذَا مِنْ تَمَامِ قِيلِ موسى لقومه .

يعني: وتذكاره إِيَّاهُمْ بِأَيَّامِ اللَّهِ، بِانْتِقَامِهِ مِنَ الْأُمَمِ الْمُكَذِّبَةِ لِلرُّسُلِ.

وَفِيمَا قَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ نَظَرٌ؛ وَالظَّاهِرُ أَنَّهُ خَبَرٌ مُسْتَأْنَفٌ مِنَ اللَّهِ تَعَالَى لِهَذِهِ الأمة، فإنه قد قيل: إِنَّ قِصَّةَ عَادٍ وَثَمُودَ لَيْسَتْ فِي التَّوْرَاةِ، فَلَوْ كَانَ هَذَا مِنْ كَلَامِ مُوسَى لِقَوْمِهِ وقَصَه عَلَيْهِمْ ذَلِكَ فَلَا شَكَّ أَنْ تَكُونَ هَاتَانِ الْقِصَّتَانِ فِي "التَّوْرَاةِ"، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ. وَبِالْجُمْلَةِ فَاللَّهُ تَعَالَى قَدْ قَصَّ عَلَيْنَا خَبَرَ قَوْمِ نُوحٍ وَعَادٍ وَثَمُودَ وَغَيْرِهِمْ مِنَ الْأُمَمِ الْمُكَذِّبَةِ لِلرُّسُلِ، مِمَّا لَا يُحْصِي عَدَدَهُمْ إِلَّا اللَّهُ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ أَتَتْهُمْ رُسُلُهُمْ بِالْبَيِّنَاتِ، أَيْ: بِالْحُجَجِ وَالدَّلَائِلِ الْوَاضِحَاتِ الْبَاهِرَاتِ الْقَاطِعَاتِ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ إِسْحَاقَ، عَنْ عَمْرِو بْنِ مَيْمُونٍ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ أَنَّهُ قَالَ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿لَا يَعْلَمُهُمْ إِلا اللَّهُ﴾ كَذَبَ النَّسَّابُونَ.

وَقَالَ عُرْوَةُ بْنُ الزُّبَيْرِ: مَا وَجَدْنَا أَحَدًا يَعْرِفُ مَا بَعْدَ مَعَدِ بْنِ عَدْنَانَ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَرَدُّوا أَيْدِيَهُمْ فِي أَفْوَاهِهِمْ﴾ اخْتَلَفَ الْمُفَسِّرُونَ فِي مَعْنَاهُ، فَقِيلَ: مَعْنَاهُ: أَنَّهُمْ أَشَارُوا إِلَى أَفْوَاهِ الرُّسُلِ يَأْمُرُونَهُمْ بِالسُّكُوتِ عَنْهُمْ، لَمَّا دَعَوْهُمْ إِلَى اللَّهِ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ.

وَقِيلَ: بَلْ وَضَعُوا أَيْدِيَهُمْ عَلَى أَفْوَاهِهِمْ تَكْذِيبًا لَهُمْ.

وَقِيلَ: بَلْ هُوَ عِبَارَةٌ عَنْ سُكُوتِهِمْ عَنْ جَوَابِ الرُّسُلِ.

وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ، وَمُحَمَّدُ بْنُ كَعْبٍ، وَقَتَادَةُ: مَعْنَاهُ: أَنَّهُمْ كَذَّبُوهُمْ وَرَدُّوا عَلَيْهِمْ قَوْلَهُمْ بِأَفْوَاهِهِمْ.

قَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: وَتَوْجِيهُهُ أَنَّ "فِي" ها هنا بِمَعْنَى "الْبَاءِ"، قَالَ: وَقَدْ سُمِعَ مِنَ الْعَرَبِ: "أَدْخَلَكَ اللَّهُ بِالْجَنَّةِ" يَعْنُونَ: فِي الْجَنَّةِ، وَقَالَ الشَّاعِرُ:

وَأَرْغَبُ فِيهَا عَن لَقيطٍ ورهْطه ... عَن سِنْبس لَسْتُ أرْغَب ...

يُرِيدُ: أَرْغَبُ بِهَا .

قُلْتُ: وَيُؤَيِّدُ قَوْلَ مُجَاهِدٍ تَفْسِيرُ ذَلِكَ بِتَمَامِ الْكَلَامِ: ﴿وَقَالُوا إِنَّا كَفَرْنَا بِمَا أُرْسِلْتُمْ بِهِ وَإِنَّا لَفِي شَكٍّ مِمَّا تَدْعُونَنَا إِلَيْهِ مُرِيبٍ﴾ فَكَأَنَّ هَذَا [وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ] تَفْسِيرٌ لِمَعْنَى رَدِّ أَيْدِيهِمْ فِي أَفْوَاهِهِمْ.

وَقَالَ سُفْيَانُ الثَّوْرِيُّ، وَإِسْرَائِيلُ، عَنْ أَبِي إِسْحَاقَ عَنْ أَبِي الْأَحْوَصِ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿فَرَدُّوا أَيْدِيَهُمْ فِي أَفْوَاهِهِمْ﴾ قَالَ: عَضُّوا عَلَيْهَا غَيْظًا.

وَقَالَ شُعْبَةُ، عَنْ أَبِي إِسْحَاقَ، أَبِي هُبَيرَْة ابْنِ مَرْيَمَ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ أَنَّهُ قَالَ ذَلِكَ أَيْضًا. وَقَدِ اخْتَارَهُ عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ، وَوَجَّهَهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ مُخْتَارًا لَهُ، بِقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى عَنِ الْمُنَافِقِينَ: ﴿وَإِذَا خَلَوْا عَضُّوا عَلَيْكُمُ الأنَامِلَ مِنَ الْغَيْظِ﴾ [آلِ عِمْرَانَ: ١١٩] .

وَقَالَ الْعَوْفِيُّ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: لَمَّا سُمِعُوا كِتَابَ اللَّهِ عَجبوا، ورجعوا بأيديهم إلى أفواههم.

وَقَالُوا: ﴿إِنَّا كَفَرْنَا بِمَا أُرْسِلْتُمْ بِهِ وَإِنَّا لَفِي شَكٍّ مِمَّا تَدْعُونَنَا إِلَيْهِ مُرِيبٍ﴾ يَقُولُونَ: لَا نُصَدِّقُكُمْ فِيمَا جِئْتُمْ بِهِ؛ فَإِنَّ عِنْدَنَا فِيهِ شَكًّا قَوِيًّا.

---

## 14:10-12 — verses 10-12 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty informs us of the disputation that took place between the disbelievers and their messengers. This is because their peoples confronted them with doubt regarding what they had brought them of the worship of God alone, without partner. So the messengers said: {Is there doubt about God}

This carries two possible meanings. The first: is there doubt about His existence, for the innate natures (fitrah) bear witness to His existence, and are formed upon acknowledgment of Him, since acknowledgment of Him is necessary in sound innate natures. But doubt and confusion may occur in some of them, so they need to reflect upon the proof that leads to His existence. This is why the messengers said to them, guiding them to the way of knowing Him, that He is {the Originator of the heavens and the earth}, who created them and brought them into being without any prior model. For the evidences of coming-into-being, creation, and subjugation are manifest upon them, and they must necessarily have a Maker, and He is God, there is no god but He, the Creator of all things, their Deity and their Sovereign.

The second meaning in their statement {Is there doubt about God} is: is there doubt about His divinity and His being uniquely deserving of worship, He being the Creator of all existing things, and none deserves worship except Him alone, without partner? For most peoples acknowledged the Maker, but worshipped along with Him other intermediaries which they supposed would benefit them or bring them nearer to God.

The messengers said to them: we call you so that He may forgive you some of your sins, meaning in the abode of the Hereafter, {and grant you reprieve until an appointed term}, meaning in this worldly life, as the Almighty said: {and that you seek forgiveness from your Lord and then turn to Him in repentance, He will grant you enjoyment, a goodly enjoyment, until an appointed term, and He will grant every possessor of merit his merit} [Hud: 3]. Then the peoples said to them, disputing regarding the position of the message, after having conceded, hypothetically, the first point. The substance of what they said was: {You are naught but men like ourselves}, meaning: how can we follow you merely on your word, when we have not seen any miracle from you? {So bring us a clear authority}, meaning a wondrous sign that we propose to you.

Their messengers said to them: {We are naught but men like you}, meaning: it is true that we are human beings like you in our humanity, {but God bestows favor upon whom He wills of His servants}, meaning with messengership and prophethood, {and it is not for us to bring you any authority}, in accordance with what you have asked, {except by God's permission}, meaning after we have asked Him and He has given us permission for that, {and in God let the believers place their trust}, meaning in all their affairs.

Then the messengers said: {And why should we not place our trust in God}, meaning: what prevents us from placing our trust in Him, when He has guided us to the straightest of paths, the clearest and most evident of them? {And we will surely be patient over the harm you have caused us}, meaning through evil speech and foolish deeds, {and in God let those who trust place their trust}.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى عَمَّا دَارَ بَيْنَ الْكُفَّارِ وَبَيْنَ رُسُلِهِمْ مِنَ الْمُجَادَلَةِ، وَذَلِكَ أَنَّ أُمَمَهُمْ لَمَّا وَاجَهُوهُمْ بِالشَّكِّ فِيمَا جَاءُوهُمْ بِهِ مِنْ عِبَادَةِ اللَّهِ وَحْدَهُ لَا شَرِيكَ لَهُ، قَالَتِ الرُّسُلُ: ﴿أَفِي اللَّهِ شَكٌّ﴾

وَهَذَا يَحْتَمِلُ شَيْئَيْنِ، أَحَدِهِمَا: أَفِي وُجُودِهِ شَكٌّ، فَإِنَّ الْفِطَرَ شَاهِدَةٌ بِوُجُودِهِ، وَمَجْبُولَةٌ عَلَى الْإِقْرَارِ بِهِ، فَإِنَّ الِاعْتِرَافَ بِهِ ضَرُورِيٌّ فِي الفطَر السَّلِيمَةِ، وَلَكِنْ قَدْ يَعْرِضُ لِبَعْضِهَا شَكٌّ وَاضْطِرَابٌ، فَتَحْتَاجُ إِلَى النَّظَرِ فِي الدَّلِيلِ الْمُوَصِّلِ إِلَى وُجُودِهِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَتْ لَهُمُ الرُّسُلُ تُرْشِدُهُمْ إِلَى طَرِيقِ مَعْرِفَتِهِ بِأَنَّهُ ﴿فَاطِرِ السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالأرْضِ﴾ الَّذِي خَلَقَهَا وَابْتَدَعَهَا عَلَى غَيْرِ مِثَالٍ سَبَقَ، فَإِنَّ شَوَاهِدَ الْحُدُوثِ وَالْخَلْقِ وَالتَّسْخِيرِ ظَاهِرٌ عَلَيْهَا، فَلَا بُدَّ لَهَا مِنْ صَانِعٍ، وَهُوَ اللَّهُ لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا هُوَ، خَالِقُ كُلِّ شَيْءٍ وَإِلَهُهُ وَمَلِيكُهُ.

وَالْمَعْنَى الثَّانِي فِي قَوْلِهِمْ: ﴿أَفِي اللَّهِ شَكٌّ﴾ أَيْ: أَفِي إِلَهِيَّتِهِ وَتَفَرُّدِهِ بِوُجُوبِ الْعِبَادَةِ لَهُ شَكٌّ، وَهُوَ الْخَالِقُ لِجَمِيعِ الْمَوْجُودَاتِ، وَلَا يَسْتَحِقُّ الْعِبَادَةَ إِلَّا هُوَ، وَحْدَهُ لَا شَرِيكَ لَهُ؛ فَإِنَّ غَالِبَ الْأُمَمِ كَانَتْ مُقِرَّةً بِالصَّانِعِ، وَلَكِنْ تَعْبُدُ مَعَهُ غَيْرَهُ مِنَ الْوَسَائِطِ الَّتِي يَظُنُّونَهَا تَنْفَعُهُمْ أَوْ تُقَرِّبُهُمْ مِنَ اللَّهِ زُلْفَى.

وَقَالَتْ لَهُمُ الرُّسُلُ: نَدْعُوكُمْ لِيَغْفِرَ لَكُمْ مِنْ ذُنُوبِكُمْ، أَيْ: فِي الدَّارِ الْآخِرَةِ، ﴿وَيُؤَخِّرَكُمْ إِلَى أَجَلٍ مُسَمًّى﴾ أَيْ: فِي الدُّنْيَا، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَأَنِ اسْتَغْفِرُوا رَبَّكُمْ ثُمَّ تُوبُوا إِلَيْهِ يُمَتِّعْكُمْ مَتَاعًا حَسَنًا إِلَى أَجَلٍ مُسَمًّى وَيُؤْتِ كُلَّ ذِي فَضْلٍ فَضْلَهُ﴾ الْآيَةَ [هُودٍ: ٣] ، فَقَالَتْ لَهُمُ الْأُمَمُ مِحَاجِّينَ فِي مَقَامِ الرِّسَالَةِ، بَعْدَ تَقْدِيرِ تَسْلِيمِهِمْ لِلْمَقَامِ الْأَوَّلِ، وَحَاصِلُ مَا قَالُوهُ: ﴿إِنْ أَنْتُمْ إِلا بَشَرٌ مِثْلُنَا﴾ أَيْ: كَيْفَ نَتَّبِعُكُمْ بِمُجَرَّدِ قَوْلِكُمْ، وَلَمَّا نَرَ مِنْكُمْ مُعْجِزَةً؟ ﴿فَأْتُونَا بِسُلْطَانٍ مُبِينٍ﴾ أَيْ: خَارِقٍ نَقْتَرِحُهُ عَلَيْكُمْ.

قَالَتْ لَهُمْ رُسُلُهُمْ: ﴿إِنْ نَحْنُ إِلا بَشَرٌ مِثْلُكُمْ﴾ أَيْ: صَحِيحٌ أَنَا بَشَرٌ مِثْلُكُمْ فِي الْبَشَرِيَّةِ ﴿وَلَكِنَّ اللَّهَ يَمُنُّ عَلَى مَنْ يَشَاءُ مِنْ عِبَادِهِ﴾ أَيْ: بِالرِّسَالَةِ وَالنُّبُوَّةِ ﴿وَمَا كَانَ لَنَا أَنْ نَأْتِيَكُمْ بِسُلْطَانٍ﴾ عَلَى وَفْقِ مَا سَأَلْتُمْ ﴿إِلا بِإِذْنِ اللَّهِ﴾ أَيْ: بَعْدَ سُؤَالِنَا إِيَّاهُ، وَإِذْنِهِ لَنَا فِي ذَلِكَ، ﴿وَعَلَى اللَّهِ فَلْيَتَوَكَّلِ الْمُؤْمِنُونَ﴾ أَيْ: فِي جَمِيعِ أُمُورِهِمْ.

ثُمَّ قَالَتِ الرُّسُلُ: ﴿وَمَا لَنَا أَلا نَتَوَكَّلَ عَلَى اللَّهِ﴾ أَيْ: وَمَا يَمْنَعُنَا مِنَ التَّوَكُّلِ عَلَيْهِ، وَقَدْ هَدَانَا لِأَقْوَمِ الطُّرُقِ وَأَوْضَحِهَا وَأَبْيَنِهَا، ﴿وَلَنَصْبِرَنَّ عَلَى مَا آذَيْتُمُونَا﴾ أَيْ: مِنَ الْكَلَامِ السَّيِّئِ، وَالْأَفْعَالِ السَّخِيفَةِ، ﴿وَعَلَى اللَّهِ فَلْيَتَوَكَّلِ الْمُتَوَكِّلُونَ﴾

---

## 14:13-17 — verses 13-17 (shared commentary)

### Translation

He, exalted, informs of what the disbelieving nations threatened their messengers with: expelling them from their land and banishing them from among them, just as the people of Shu'ayb said to him and to those who believed with him: {We will surely drive you out, O Shu'ayb, and those who have believed with you, from our town, or you must return to our religion} [al-A'raf: 88]. And the people of Lot said: {Expel the family of Lot from your town; indeed they are people who keep themselves pure} [al-Naml: 56]. And He, exalted, said informing of the polytheists of Quraysh: {And indeed they were about to drive you out from the land to expel you therefrom, and then they would not have remained after you except for a little} [al-Isra: 76]. And He, exalted, said: {And when those who disbelieved plotted against you to restrain you, kill you, or expel you. They planned, and Allah planned, and Allah is the best of planners} [al-Anfal: 30].

Among His doings, exalted, was that He made His Messenger manifest and gave him victory, and made for him, by reason of his going out from Mecca, helpers and supporters and an army who fought in the path of Allah. He did not cease to raise him, exalted, from one stage to another until He opened for him Mecca, the very city that had expelled him, and established him firmly in it, and humbled the noses of his enemies among them and among the rest of the people of the earth, until people entered the religion of Allah in multitudes, and the word of Allah and His religion prevailed over all other religions, in the easts of the earth and its wests, in the shortest span of time. For this reason He, exalted, said: {So their Lord revealed to them: We will surely destroy the wrongdoers, and We will surely settle you in the land after them}, just as He, exalted, said: {And Our word has already preceded for Our servants, the messengers, that they would surely be the ones given victory, and that Our soldiers would surely be the predominant ones} [al-Saffat: 171-173]. And He, exalted, said: {Allah has decreed: I will surely overcome, I and My messengers. Indeed, Allah is Strong and Mighty} [al-Mujadalah: 21]. And He said: {And We have already written in the Zabur (Psalms) after the Reminder that the land is inherited by My righteous servants} [al-Anbiya: 105]. {Moses said to his people: Seek help through Allah and be patient. Indeed, the earth belongs to Allah; He causes to inherit it whom He wills of His servants, and the final outcome is for the righteous} [al-A'raf: 128]. And He, exalted, said: {And We caused the people who had been oppressed to inherit the eastern regions of the land and the western ones, which We had blessed. And the good word of your Lord was fulfilled for the Children of Israel because of what they had patiently endured. And We destroyed what Pharaoh and his people had built and what they had erected} [al-A'raf: 137].

His saying: {That is for whoever fears My position and fears My threat}, meaning: this threat of Mine is for whoever fears standing before Me on the Day of Resurrection, and fears My threat, which is My warning and My punishment, just as He, exalted, said: {As for he who transgressed and preferred the worldly life, then indeed, the Hellfire, that is the refuge. But as for he who feared the standing before his Lord and restrained the soul from [unlawful] desire, then indeed, Paradise, that is the refuge} [al-Nazi'at: 37-41]. And He said: {And for he who fears the standing before his Lord are two gardens} [al-Rahman: 46].

His saying: {And they sought victory}, meaning: the messengers sought help from their Lord against their people. This was said by Ibn Abbas, Mujahid, and Qatadah.

And Abd al-Rahman ibn Zayd ibn Aslam said: the nations sought a judgment against themselves, just as they said: {O Allah, if this is indeed the truth from You, then rain down upon us stones from the sky or bring us a painful punishment} [al-Anfal: 32].

It is possible that both meanings are intended, just as they sought a decisive judgment against themselves on the day of Badr, and the Messenger of Allah ﷺ also sought victory and help, and Allah, exalted, said to the polytheists: {If you sought a decision, then the decision has come to you, and if you cease [hostilities], it is best for you} to the end of the verse [al-Anfal: 19]. And Allah knows best.

{And every obstinate tyrant failed}, meaning: one who is arrogant in himself and stubbornly opposes the truth, just as He, exalted, said: {[saying], "Throw into Hell every obstinate disbeliever, preventer of good, transgressor and doubter, who made with Allah another deity; then throw him into the severe punishment"} [Qaf: 24-26].

And in the hadith: "Hellfire will be brought on the Day of Resurrection, and it will call out to the creation, saying: I have been entrusted with every obstinate tyrant." The hadith continues.

He failed and was ruined when the prophets strove earnestly in supplication to their Lord, the Mighty, the All-Powerful.

His saying: {Before him is Hell}. "Wara'" (behind) here carries the meaning of "in front of," just as He, exalted, said: {And there was in front of them a king who seized every ship by force} [al-Kahf: 79]. Ibn Abbas used to recite it as "and there was in front of them a king."

That is: in front of the obstinate tyrant is Hell, meaning: it lies in wait for him, and he will dwell in it eternally on the Day of Return, and he will be exposed to it morning and evening until the Day of Mutual Calling.

{And he is given to drink from purulent water}, meaning: in the Fire he has no drink except from scalding water or foul discharge. This one is at the extreme of heat, and that one is at the extreme of coldness and foulness, just as He said: {This, so let them taste it: scalding water and purulent discharge, and other [punishments] of its type, [in various] kinds} [Sad: 57, 58].

Mujahid and Ikrimah said: "sadid" (purulent discharge) is from pus and blood.

Qatadah said: it is what flows from his flesh and skin. And in another report from him: sadid is what comes out from the interior of the disbeliever, mixed with pus and blood.

From the hadith of Shahr ibn Hawshab, from Asma bint Yazid ibn al-Sakan, who said: I said, "O Messenger of Allah, what is tinat al-khabal (the fetid clay)?" He said: "The purulent discharge of the people of the Fire." And in another version: "the pressed-out fluid of the people of the Fire."

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Abu Umamah, may Allah be pleased with him, narrated from the Prophet ﷺ concerning His saying: {And he is given to drink from purulent water which he gulps down bit by bit}, that he said: "It is brought near to him and he detests it. When it is brought close to him, it roasts his face, and the skin of his scalp falls off. And when he drinks it, it cuts through his intestines until it comes out from his rear. Allah, exalted, says: {And they are given to drink scalding water that cuts through their intestines} [Muhammad: 15], and He says: {And if they call for relief, they will be relieved with water like murky oil that scalds the faces. Wretched is the drink} [al-Kahf: 29]."

And thus Ibn Jarir narrated it, from the hadith of Abdullah ibn al-Mubarak, with this chain. And he and Ibn Abi Hatim also narrated it from the hadith of Baqiyyah ibn al-Walid, from Safwan ibn Amr, with this chain.

His saying: {He gulps it down bit by bit}, meaning: he swallows it with difficulty and detests it, that is, he drinks it under compulsion and force. He does not put it in his mouth until the angel strikes him with an iron club, just as He, exalted, said: {And for them are hooked rods of iron} [al-Hajj: 21].

{And he can hardly swallow it}, meaning: he can hardly gulp it down because of its foul color, taste, and smell, and its unbearable heat or coldness.

{And death approaches him from every side}, meaning: his entire body, limbs, and organs suffer pain because of it.

Maymun ibn Mihran said: from every bone, vein, and sinew.

Ikrimah said: even from the very tips of his hair.

Ibrahim al-Taymi said: from the place of every hair, that is, from his body, even from the tips of his hair.

Ibn Jarir said: {And death approaches him from every side}, meaning: from in front of him and behind him, from his right and his left, from above him and from beneath his feet, and from all the rest of the parts of his body.

Al-Dahhak said, from Ibn Abbas: {And death approaches him from every side}, he said: this refers to the various types of punishment with which Allah punishes him on the Day of Resurrection in the fire of Hell, and there is not a single type of it but that death would come to him from it, if it were the case that he could die, but he does not die. Because Allah, exalted, said: {It will not be decreed for them to die, nor will its punishment be lightened for them. Thus do We recompense every ungrateful one} [Fatir: 36].

The meaning of Ibn Abbas's statement, may Allah be pleased with him, is that there is no type among these types of punishment but that, when it comes upon him, would necessitate that he die from it, if it were possible for him to die, but he does not die, so that he remains eternally in continuous punishment and torment. For this reason He said: {And death approaches him from every side, but he is not to die}.

His saying: {And beyond him is a harsh punishment}, meaning: after this condition there is for him another punishment, harsh, that is, painful, difficult, severe, harsher than what preceded it and more calamitous and bitter. This is like what He, exalted, said about the tree of Zaqqum: {Indeed, it is a tree that grows in the bottom of the Hellfire, its emerging fruit as if it was the heads of devils. And indeed, they will eat from it and fill with it their bellies. Then indeed, they will have after it a mixture of scalding water. Then indeed, their return will be to the Hellfire} [al-Saffat: 64-68]. He informs that at times they will be eating Zaqqum, and at times drinking scalding water, and at times they will be returned to the Hellfire. We seek refuge with Allah from that. And likewise He, exalted, said: {This is Hell, which the criminals deny. They will circulate between it and scalding water, heated to the utmost} [al-Rahman: 43, 44]. And He, exalted, said: {Indeed, the tree of Zaqqum is food for the sinful, like murky oil, boiling within the bellies like the boiling of scalding water. [It will be said], "Seize him and drag him into the midst of the Hellfire. Then pour over his head from the punishment of scalding water." "Taste! Indeed, you are the mighty, the noble!" "Indeed, this is what you used to doubt"} [al-Dukhan: 43-50]. And He said: {And the companions of the left, what are the companions of the left? [They will be] in scorching wind and scalding water, and a shade of black smoke, neither cool nor beneficial} [al-Waqi'ah: 41-44]. And He, exalted, said: {This [is so]. And indeed, for the transgressors is the worst return: Hell, they will burn therein, and wretched is the resting place. This, so let them taste it: scalding water and purulent discharge, and other [punishments] of its type, [in various] kinds} [Sad: 55-58]. And so on with other verses indicating the variety of punishment upon them, its repetition, its kinds and forms, which none can enumerate except Allah, mighty and majestic, as a fitting recompense. {And your Lord is not ever unjust to His servants} [Fussilat: 46].

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى عَمَّا تَوَعَّدَتْ بِهِ الْأُمَمُ الْكَافِرَةُ رُسُلَهُمْ، مِنَ الْإِخْرَاجِ مَنْ أَرْضِهِمْ، وَالنَّفْيِ مِنْ بَيْنِ أَظْهُرِهِمْ، كَمَا قَالَ قَوْمُ شُعَيْبٍ لَهُ وَلِمَنْ آمَنَ بِهِ: ﴿لَنُخْرِجَنَّكَ يَا شُعَيْبُ وَالَّذِينَ آمَنُوا مَعَكَ مِنْ قَرْيَتِنَا أَوْ لَتَعُودُنَّ فِي مِلَّتِنَا﴾ [الْأَعْرَافِ: ٨٨] ، وَقَالَ قَوْمُ لُوطٍ: ﴿أَخْرِجُوا آلَ لُوطٍ مِنْ قَرْيَتِكُمْ إِنَّهُمْ أُنَاسٌ يَتَطَهَّرُونَ﴾ [النَّمْلِ: ٥٦] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى إِخْبَارًا عَنْ مُشْرِكِي قُرَيْشٍ: ﴿وَإِنْ كَادُوا لَيَسْتَفِزُّونَكَ مِنَ الأرْضِ لِيُخْرِجُوكَ مِنْهَا وَإِذًا لَا يَلْبَثُونَ خِلافَكَ إِلا قَلِيلا﴾ [الْإِسْرَاءِ: ٧٦] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَإِذْ يَمْكُرُ بِكَ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا لِيُثْبِتُوكَ أَوْ يَقْتُلُوكَ أَوْ يُخْرِجُوكَ وَيَمْكُرُونَ وَيَمْكُرُ اللَّهُ وَاللَّهُ خَيْرُ الْمَاكِرِينَ﴾ [الْأَنْفَالِ: ٣٠] .

وَكَانَ مِنْ صُنْعِهِ تَعَالَى: أَنَّهُ أَظْهَرَ رَسُولَهُ وَنَصَرَهُ، وَجَعَلَ لَهُ بِسَبَبِ خُرُوجِهِ مِنْ مَكَّةَ أَنْصَارًا وَأَعْوَانًا وَجُنْدًا، يُقَاتِلُونَ فِي سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ، وَلَمْ يَزَلْ يُرَقِّيهِ [اللَّهُ] تَعَالَى مِنْ شَيْءٍ إِلَى شَيْءٍ، حَتَّى فَتَحَ لَهُ مَكَّةَ الَّتِي أَخْرَجَتْهُ، وَمَكَّنَ لَهُ فِيهَا، وَأَرْغَمَ آنَافَ أَعْدَائِهِ مِنْهُمْ، و [مِنْ] سَائِرِ [أَهْلِ] الْأَرْضِ، حَتَّى دَخَلَ النَّاسُ فِي دِينِ اللَّهِ أَفْوَاجًا، وَظَهَرَتْ كَلِمَةُ اللَّهِ وَدِينُهُ عَلَى سَائِرِ الْأَدْيَانِ، فِي مَشَارِقِ الْأَرْضِ وَمَغَارِبِهَا فِي أَيْسَرِ زَمَانٍ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿فَأَوْحَى إِلَيْهِمْ رَبُّهُمْ لَنُهْلِكَنَّ الظَّالِمِينَ وَلَنُسْكِنَنَّكُمُ الأرْضَ مِنْ بَعْدِهِمْ﴾ كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلَقَدْ سَبَقَتْ كَلِمَتُنَا لِعِبَادِنَا الْمُرْسَلِينَ إِنَّهُمْ لَهُمُ الْمَنْصُورُونَ وَإِنَّ جُنْدَنَا لَهُمُ الْغَالِبُونَ﴾ [الصَّافَّاتِ: ١٧١ -١٧٣] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿كَتَبَ اللَّهُ لأغْلِبَنَّ أَنَا وَرُسُلِي إِنَّ اللَّهَ قَوِيٌّ عَزِيزٌ﴾ [الْمُجَادَلَةِ: ٢١] ، وَقَالَ: ﴿وَلَقَدْ كَتَبْنَا فِي الزَّبُورِ مِنْ بَعْدِ الذِّكْرِ أَنَّ الأرْضَ يَرِثُهَا عِبَادِيَ الصَّالِحُونَ﴾ [الأنبياء: ١٠٥] ، ﴿قَالَ مُوسَى لِقَوْمِهِ اسْتَعِينُوا بِاللَّهِ وَاصْبِرُوا إِنَّ الأرْضَ لِلَّهِ يُورِثُهَا مَنْ يَشَاءُ مِنْ عِبَادِهِ وَالْعَاقِبَةُ لِلْمُتَّقِينَ﴾ [الْأَعْرَافِ: ١٢٨] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَأَوْرَثْنَا الْقَوْمَ الَّذِينَ كَانُوا يُسْتَضْعَفُونَ مَشَارِقَ الأرْضِ وَمَغَارِبَهَا الَّتِي بَارَكْنَا فِيهَا وَتَمَّتْ كَلِمَةُ رَبِّكَ الْحُسْنَى عَلَى بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ بِمَا صَبَرُوا وَدَمَّرْنَا مَا كَانَ يَصْنَعُ فِرْعَوْنُ وَقَوْمُهُ وَمَا كَانُوا يَعْرِشُونَ﴾ [الْأَعْرَافِ: ١٣٧] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿ذَلِكَ لِمَنْ خَافَ مَقَامِي وَخَافَ وَعِيدِ﴾ أَيْ: وَعِيدِي هَذَا لِمَنْ خَافَ مَقَامِي بَيْنَ يَدَيْ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ، وَخَشِيَ مِنْ وَعِيدِي، وَهُوَ تَخْوِيفِي وَعَذَابِي، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿فَأَمَّا مَنْ طَغَى وَآثَرَ الْحَيَاةَ الدُّنْيَا فَإِنَّ الْجَحِيمَ هِيَ الْمَأْوَى وَأَمَّا مَنْ خَافَ مَقَامَ رَبِّهِ وَنَهَى النَّفْسَ عَنِ الْهَوَى فَإِنَّ الْجَنَّةَ هِيَ الْمَأْوَى﴾ [النَّازِعَاتِ: ٣٧ -٤١] ، وَقَالَ: ﴿وَلِمَنْ خَافَ مَقَامَ رَبِّهِ جَنَّتَانِ﴾ [الرَّحْمَنِ: ٤٦] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَاسْتَفْتَحُوا﴾ أَيِ: اسْتَنْصَرَتِ الرُّسُلُ رَبَّهَا عَلَى قَوْمِهَا. قَالَهُ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ، وَمُجَاهِدٌ، وَقَتَادَةُ.

وَقَالَ عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ: اسْتَفْتَحَتِ الْأُمَمُ عَلَى أَنْفُسِهَا، كَمَا قَالُوا: ﴿اللَّهُمَّ إِنْ كَانَ هَذَا هُوَ الْحَقَّ مِنْ عِنْدِكَ فَأَمْطِرْ عَلَيْنَا حِجَارَةً مِنَ السَّمَاءِ أَوِ ائْتِنَا بِعَذَابٍ أَلِيمٍ﴾ [الْأَنْفَالِ: ٣٢] .

وَيُحْتَمَلُ أَنْ يَكُونَ هَذَا مُرَادًا وَهَذَا مُرَادًا، كَمَا أَنَّهُمُ اسْتَفْتَحُوا عَلَى أَنْفُسِهِمْ يَوْمَ بَدْرٍ، وَاسْتَفْتَحَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ وَاسْتَنْصَرَ، وَقَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى لِلْمُشْرِكِينَ: ﴿إِنْ تَسْتَفْتِحُوا فَقَدْ جَاءَكُمُ الْفَتْحُ وَإِنْ تَنْتَهُوا فَهُوَ خَيْرٌ لَكُمْ﴾ الْآيَةَ [الْأَنْفَالِ: ١٩] ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

﴿وَخَابَ كُلُّ جَبَّارٍ عَنِيدٍ﴾ أَيْ: مُتَجَبِّرٌ فِي نَفْسِهِ مُعَانِدٌ لِلْحَقِّ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿أَلْقِيَا فِي جَهَنَّمَ كُلَّ كَفَّارٍ عَنِيدٍ مَنَّاعٍ لِلْخَيْرِ مُعْتَدٍ مُرِيبٍ الَّذِي جَعَلَ مَعَ اللَّهِ إِلَهًا آخَرَ فَأَلْقِيَاهُ فِي الْعَذَابِ الشَّدِيدِ﴾ [ق: ٢٤ -٢٦] .

وَفِي الْحَدِيثِ: "إِنَّهُ يُؤْتَى بِجَهَنَّمَ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ، فَتُنَادِي الْخَلَائِقَ فَتَقُولُ: إِنِّي وُكلت بِكُلِّ جَبَّارٍ عَنِيدٍ" الْحَدِيثَ .

خَابَ وَخَسِرَ حِينَ اجْتَهَدَ الْأَنْبِيَاءَ فِي الِابْتِهَالِ إِلَى رَبِّهَا الْعَزِيزِ الْمُقْتَدِرِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿مِنْ وَرَائِهِ جَهَنَّمُ﴾ وَ"وراء" ها هنا بِمَعْنَى "أَمَامُ"، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَكَانَ وَرَاءَهُمْ مَلِكٌ يَأْخُذُ كُلَّ سَفِينَةٍ غَصْبًا﴾ [الْكَهْفِ: ٧٩] ، وَكَانَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ يَقْرَؤُهَا "وَكَانَ أَمَامَهُمْ مَلِكٌ".

أَيْ: مِنْ وَرَاءِ الْجَبَّارِ الْعَنِيدِ جَهَنَّمُ، أَيْ: هِيَ لَهُ بِالْمِرْصَادِ، يَسْكُنُهَا مُخَلَّدًا يَوْمَ الْمَعَادِ، وَيُعْرَضُ عليها غدوا وعشيا إلى يوم التناد.

﴿وَيُسْقَى مِنْ مَاءٍ صَدِيدٍ﴾ أَيْ: فِي النَّارِ لَيْسَ لَهُ شَرَابٌ إِلَّا مِنْ حَمِيمٍ أَوْ غَسَّاقٍ، فَهَذَا فِي غَايَةِ الْحَرَارَةِ، وَهَذَا فِي غَايَةِ الْبَرْدِ وَالنَّتَنِ، كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿هَذَا فَلْيَذُوقُوهُ حَمِيمٌ وَغَسَّاقٌ وَآخَرُ مِنْ شَكْلِهِ أَزْوَاجٌ﴾ [ص: ٥٧، ٥٨] .

وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ، وَعِكْرِمَةُ: الصَّدِيدُ: مِنَ الْقَيْحِ وَالدَّمِ.

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: هُوَ مَا يُسِيلُ مِنْ لَحْمِهِ وَجِلْدِهِ. وَفِي رِوَايَةٍ عَنْهُ: الصَّدِيدُ: مَا يَخْرُجُ مِنْ جَوْفِ الْكَافِرِ، قَدْ خَالَطَ الْقَيْحَ وَالدَّمَ.

وَمِنْ حَدِيثِ شَهْر بْنِ حَوْشَب، عَنْ أَسْمَاءَ بِنْتِ يَزِيدَ بْنِ السَّكَنِ قَالَتْ: قُلْتُ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، مَا طِينَةُ الْخَبَالِ؟ قَالَ: "صَدِيدُ أَهْلِ النَّارِ" وَفِي رِوَايَةٍ: "عُصَارة أَهْلِ النَّارِ" .

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا عَلِيُّ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ، أَنْبَأَنَا عَبْدُ اللَّهِ، أَنَا صَفْوَانُ بْنُ عَمْرٍو، عَنْ عُبَيْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ بُرْ، عَنْ أَبِي أُمَامَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَيُسْقَى مِنْ مَاءٍ صَدِيدٍ يَتَجَرَّعُهُ﴾ قَالَ: "يُقَرَّبُ إِلَيْهِ فَيَتَكَرَّهُهُ، فَإِذَا أُدْنِيَ مِنْهُ شَوى وَجْهَهُ، وَوَقَعَتْ فَرْوَةُ رَأْسِهِ، فَإِذَا شَرِبَهُ قَطَّعَ أَمْعَاءَهُ حَتَّى يَخْرُجَ مِنْ دُبُرِهِ. يَقُولُ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى ﴿وَسُقُوا مَاءً حَمِيمًا فَقَطَّعَ أَمْعَاءَهُمْ﴾ [مُحَمَّدٍ: ١٥] ، وَيَقُولُ: ﴿وَإِنْ يَسْتَغِيثُوا يُغَاثُوا بِمَاءٍ كَالْمُهْلِ يَشْوِي الْوُجُوهَ بِئْسَ الشَّرَابُ﴾ [الْكَهْفِ: ٢٩] .

وَهَكَذَا رَوَاهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ الْمُبَارَكِ، بِهِ وَرَوَاهُ هُوَ وابن أبي حاتم: من حديث بَقِيَّة ابن الْوَلِيدِ، عَنْ صَفْوَانَ بْنِ عَمْرٍو، بِهِ .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿يَتَجَرَّعُهُ﴾ أَيْ: يَتَغَصَّصُهُ وَيَتَكَرَّهُهُ، أَيْ: يَشْرَبُهُ قَهْرًا وَقَسْرًا، لَا يَضَعُهُ فِي فِيهِ حَتَّى يَضْرِبَهُ الْمَلَكُ بِمِطْرَاقٍ مِنْ حَدِيدٍ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلَهُمْ مَقَامِعُ مِنْ حَدِيدٍ﴾ [الْحَجِّ: ٢١] .

﴿وَلا يَكَادُ يُسِيغُهُ﴾ أَيْ: يَزْدَرِدُهُ لِسُوءِ لَوْنِهِ وَطَعْمِهِ وَرِيحِهِ، وَحَرَارَتِهِ أَوْ بَرْدِهِ الَّذِي لَا يُسْتَطَاعُ.

﴿وَيَأْتِيهِ الْمَوْتُ مِنْ كُلِّ مَكَانٍ﴾ أَيْ: يَأْلَمُ لَهُ جَمِيعُ بَدَنِهِ وَجَوَارِحِهِ وَأَعْضَائِهِ.

قَالَ مَيْمُونُ بْنُ مِهْرَان: مِنْ كُلِّ عَظْمٍ، وَعِرْقٍ، وَعَصَبٍ.

وَقَالَ عكرمة: حتى من أطراف شعره.

وَقَالَ إِبْرَاهِيمُ التَّيْمِيُّ: مِنْ مَوْضِعِ كُلِّ شَعْرَةٍ، أَيْ: مِنْ جَسَدِهِ، حَتَّى مِنْ أَطْرَافِ شَعْرِهِ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: ﴿وَيَأْتِيهِ الْمَوْتُ مِنْ كُلِّ مَكَانٍ﴾ أَيْ: مِنْ أَمَامِهِ وَوَرَائِهِ، وَعَنْ يَمِينِهِ وَشِمَالِهِ، وَمِنْ فَوْقِهِ وَمِنْ تَحْتِ أَرْجُلِهِ وَمِنْ سَائِرِ أَعْضَاءِ جَسَدِهِ.

وَقَالَ الضَّحَّاكُ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿وَيَأْتِيهِ الْمَوْتُ مِنْ كُلِّ مَكَانٍ﴾ قَالَ: أَنْوَاعُ الْعَذَابِ الَّذِي يُعَذِّبُهُ اللَّهُ بِهَا يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ فِي نَارِ جَهَنَّمَ، وَلَيْسَ مِنْهَا نَوْعٌ إِلَّا الْمَوْتُ يَأْتِيهِ مِنْهُ لَوْ كَانَ يَمُوتُ، وَلَكِنْ لَا يَمُوتُ؛ لَأَنَّ اللَّهَ تَعَالَى قَالَ: ﴿لَا يُقْضَى عَلَيْهِمْ فَيَمُوتُوا وَلا يُخَفَّفُ عَنْهُمْ مِنْ عَذَابِهَا [كَذَلِكَ نَجْزِي كُلَّ كَفُورٍ] ﴾ [فَاطِرٍ: ٣٦] .

وَمَعْنَى كَلَامِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ: أَنَّهُ مَا مِنْ نَوْعٍ مِنْ هَذِهِ الْأَنْوَاعِ مِنْ [هَذَا] الْعَذَابِ إِلَّا إِذَا وَرَدَ عَلَيْهِ اقْتَضَى أَنْ يَمُوتَ مِنْهُ لَوْ كَانَ يَمُوتُ، وَلَكِنَّهُ لَا يَمُوتُ لِيَخْلُدَ فِي دَوَامِ الْعَذَابِ وَالنَّكَالِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿وَيَأْتِيهِ الْمَوْتُ مِنْ كُلِّ مَكَانٍ وَمَا هُوَ بِمَيِّتٍ﴾

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَمِنْ وَرَائِهِ عَذَابٌ غَلِيظٌ﴾ أَيْ: وَلَهُ مِنْ بَعْدِ هَذَا الْحَالِ عَذَابٌ آخَرُ غَلِيظٌ، أَيْ: مُؤْلِمٌ صَعْبٌ شَدِيدٌ أَغْلَظُ مِنَ الَّذِي قَبْلَهُ وَأَدْهَى وَأَمَرُّ. وَهَذَا كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى عَنْ شَجَرَةِ الزَّقُّومِ: ﴿إِنَّهَا شَجَرَةٌ تَخْرُجُ فِي أَصْلِ الْجَحِيمِ طَلْعُهَا كَأَنَّهُ رُءُوسُ الشَّيَاطِينِ فَإِنَّهُمْ لآكِلُونَ مِنْهَا فَمَالِئُونَ مِنْهَا الْبُطُونَ ثُمَّ إِنَّ لَهُمْ عَلَيْهَا لَشَوْبًا مِنْ حَمِيمٍ ثُمَّ إِنَّ مَرْجِعَهُمْ لإلَى الْجَحِيمِ﴾ [الصَّافَّاتِ: ٦٤ -٦٨] ، فَأَخْبَرَ أَنَّهُمْ تَارَةً يَكُونُونَ فِي أَكْلِ زَقُّومٍ، وَتَارَةً فِي شُرْبِ حَمِيمٍ، وَتَارَةً يُرَدُّونَ إِلَى الْجَحِيمِ عِيَاذًا بِاللَّهِ مِنْ ذَلِكَ، وَهَكَذَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿هَذِهِ جَهَنَّمُ الَّتِي يُكَذِّبُ بِهَا الْمُجْرِمُونَ يَطُوفُونَ بَيْنَهَا وَبَيْنَ حَمِيمٍ آنٍ﴾ [الرَّحْمَنِ: ٤٣، ٤٤] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿إِنَّ شَجَرَةَ الزَّقُّومِ طَعَامُ الأثِيمِ كَالْمُهْلِ يَغْلِي فِي الْبُطُونِ كَغَلْيِ الْحَمِيمِ خُذُوهُ فَاعْتِلُوهُ إِلَى سَوَاءِ الْجَحِيمِ ثُمَّ صُبُّوا فَوْقَ رَأْسِهِ مِنْ عَذَابِ الْحَمِيمِ ذُقْ إِنَّكَ أَنْتَ الْعَزِيزُ الْكَرِيمُ إِنَّ هَذَا مَا كُنْتُمْ بِهِ تَمْتَرُونَ﴾ [الدُّخَانِ: ٤٣ -٥٠] ، وَقَالَ: ﴿وَأَصْحَابُ الشِّمَالِ مَا أَصْحَابُ الشِّمَالِ فِي سَمُومٍ وَحَمِيمٍ وَظِلٍّ مِنْ يَحْمُومٍ لَا بَارِدٍ وَلا كَرِيمٍ﴾ [الْوَاقِعَةِ: ٤١ -٤٤] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿هَذَا وَإِنَّ لِلطَّاغِينَ لَشَرَّ مَآبٍ جَهَنَّمَ يَصْلَوْنَهَا فَبِئْسَ الْمِهَادُ هَذَا فَلْيَذُوقُوهُ حَمِيمٌ وَغَسَّاقٌ وَآخَرُ مِنْ شَكْلِهِ أَزْوَاجٌ﴾ [ص: ٥٥ -٥٨] ، إِلَى غَيْرِ ذَلِكَ مِنَ الْآيَاتِ الدَّالَّةِ عَلَى تَنَوُّعِ الْعَذَابِ عَلَيْهِمْ، وَتَكْرَارِهِ وَأَنْوَاعِهِ وَأَشْكَالِهِ، مِمَّا لَا يُحْصِيهِ إِلَّا اللَّهُ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، جَزَاءً وِفَاقًا، ﴿وَمَا رَبُّكَ بِظَلامٍ لِلْعَبِيدِ﴾ [فُصِّلَتْ: ٤٦] .

---

## 14:18 — verse 18

### Translation

This is a parable that God Almighty gave for the deeds of the disbelievers who worshipped others besides God, denied His messengers, and built their deeds upon no sound foundation. So those deeds collapsed and they found themselves without them at the very moment they needed them most. God Almighty says: {The parable of those who disbelieved in their Lord: their deeds}, meaning, the parable of the deeds of those who disbelieved, on the Day of Resurrection, when they seek their reward from God Almighty. For they used to reckon that they were upon something, but they found nothing, and they did not obtain any result except like what results from ashes when a violent, raging wind strikes them: {on a stormy day}, meaning, a day with a strong, raging wind. So they will not be able to do anything with the deeds they earned in the worldly life, just as they would not be able to gather up these ashes on such a day. As God Almighty says: {And We shall turn to whatever deeds they did and make them scattered dust} [al-Furqan: 23]. And God Almighty says: {The parable of what they spend in this worldly life is like the parable of a wind containing bitter cold that strikes the tilth of a people who wronged themselves, and destroys it} [Al Imran: 117]. And God Almighty says: {O you who believe, do not nullify your charities with reminders of your generosity and with insult, like the one who spends his wealth to be seen by people and does not believe in God and the Last Day. His parable is like that of a smooth rock covered with soil, then a downpour strikes it and leaves it bare. They have no power over anything they have earned. And God does not guide the disbelieving people} [al-Baqarah: 264].

And He says in this verse: {That is the far straying}, meaning, their striving and their deeds rested on no foundation and no soundness, until they lost their reward at the very moment they needed it most. {That is the far straying}.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

هَذَا مَثَلٌ ضَرَبَهُ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى لِأَعْمَالِ الْكُفَّارِ الَّذِينَ عَبَدُوا مَعَ الله غيره، وكذبوا رسله، وبنوا أعمالهم عَلَى غَيْرِ أَسَاسٍ صَحِيحٍ؛ فَانْهَارَتْ وعَدِمُوها أَحْوَجَ مَا كَانُوا إِلَيْهَا، فَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿مَثَلُ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا بِرَبِّهِمْ أَعْمَالُهُمْ﴾ أَيْ: مَثَلُ أَعْمَالِ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ إِذَا طَلَبُوا ثَوَابَهَا مِنَ اللَّهِ تَعَالَى؛ لِأَنَّهُمْ كَانُوا يَحْسَبُونَ أَنَّهُمْ عَلَى شَيْءٍ، فَلَمْ يَجِدُوا شَيْئًا، وَلَا أَلْفَوْا حَاصِلًا إِلَّا كَمَا يتحصَّل مِنَ الرَّمَادِ إِذَا اشْتَدَّتْ بِهِ الرِّيحُ الْعَاصِفَةُ ﴿فِي يَوْمٍ عَاصِفٍ﴾ أَيْ: ذِي رِيحٍ عَاصِفَةٍ قَوِيَّةٍ، فَلَا [يَقْدِرُونَ عَلَى شَيْءٍ مِنْ أَعْمَالِهِمُ الَّتِي كَسَبُوهَا فِي الدُّنْيَا إِلَّا كَمَا] يَقْدِرُونَ عَلَى جَمْعِ هَذَا الرَّمَادِ فِي هَذَا الْيَوْمِ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَقَدِمْنَا إِلَى مَا عَمِلُوا مِنْ عَمَلٍ فَجَعَلْنَاهُ هَبَاءً مَنْثُورًا﴾ [الْفُرْقَانِ: ٢٣] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿مَثَلُ مَا يُنْفِقُونَ فِي هَذِهِ الْحَيَاةِ الدُّنْيَا كَمَثَلِ رِيحٍ فِيهَا صِرٌّ أَصَابَتْ حَرْثَ قَوْمٍ ظَلَمُوا أَنْفُسَهُمْ فَأَهْلَكَتْهُ﴾ [آلِ عِمْرَانَ: ١١٧] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا لَا تُبْطِلُوا صَدَقَاتِكُمْ بِالْمَنِّ وَالأذَى كَالَّذِي يُنْفِقُ مَالَهُ رِئَاءَ النَّاسِ وَلا يُؤْمِنُ بِاللَّهِ وَالْيَوْمِ الآخِرِ فَمَثَلُهُ كَمَثَلِ صَفْوَانٍ عَلَيْهِ تُرَابٌ فَأَصَابَهُ وَابِلٌ فَتَرَكَهُ صَلْدًا لَا يَقْدِرُونَ عَلَى شَيْءٍ مِمَّا كَسَبُوا وَاللَّهُ لَا يَهْدِي الْقَوْمَ الْكَافِرِينَ﴾ [الْبَقَرَةِ: ٢٦٤] .

وَقَالَ فِي هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ: ﴿ذَلِكَ هُوَ الضَّلالُ الْبَعِيدُ﴾ أَيْ: سَعْيُهُمْ وَعَمَلُهُمْ عَلَى غَيْرِ أَسَاسٍ وَلَا اسْتِقَامَةٍ حَتَّى فَقَدُوا ثَوَابَهُمْ أَحْوَجَ مَا هُمْ إِلَيْهِ، ﴿ذَلِكَ هُوَ الضَّلالُ الْبَعِيدُ﴾ .

---

## 14:19-20 — verses 19-20 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Most High says, informing of His power over the return of bodies on the Day of Resurrection, that He created the heavens and the earth, which are greater than the creation of mankind. Is not He who had power to create these heavens, in their height, vastness, and magnitude, and what is in them of fixed stars and moving planets, and varied motions, and dazzling signs, and this earth with what is in it of level plains and low valleys and mountains firmly set like pegs, and wildernesses and deserts and barren lands, and seas and trees, and plants and animals in their differing kinds and benefits, forms and colors, is not such a One able to do what He wills? {Have they not seen that Allah, who created the heavens and the earth and did not tire from creating them, is able to give life to the dead? Yes indeed, He is over all things capable} [al-Ahqaf: 33]. And the Most High says: {Does man not consider that We created him from a sperm-drop, and behold, he is an open disputant, and he coins for Us a similitude and forgets his own creation, saying: Who will give life to the bones when they have decayed? Say: He will give them life who produced them the first time, and He is knowing of all creation. He who made for you fire from the green tree, and behold, you kindle from it. Is not He who created the heavens and the earth able to create the like of them? Yes indeed, and He is the Supreme Creator, the All-Knowing. His command, when He wills a thing, is only to say to it "Be," and it is. So glory be to Him in whose hand is the dominion of all things, and to Him you will be returned} [Ya-Sin: 77-83].

And His saying: {If He wills, He can do away with you and bring a new creation, and that is not difficult for Allah}, meaning: it is not something great or impossible for Him, rather it is easy for Him, if you oppose His command, to remove you and bring others of a different description than yours, as the Most High says: {O mankind, you are those in need of Allah, while Allah is the Self-Sufficient, the Praiseworthy. If He wills, He can do away with you and bring a new creation, and that is not difficult for Allah} [Fatir: 15-17]. And He says: {And if you turn away, He will replace you with another people, then they will not be like you} [Muhammad: 38]. And He says: {O you who believe, whoever among you turns back from his religion, then Allah will bring a people whom He loves and who love Him} [al-Ma'idah: 54]. And He says: {If He wills, He can do away with you, O mankind, and bring others, and Allah is ever able to do that} [al-Nisa: 133].

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُخْبِرًا عَنْ قُدْرَتِهِ عَلَى مَعَادِ الْأَبْدَانِ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ، بِأَنَّهُ خَلَقَ السَّمَوَاتِ وَالْأَرْضَ الَّتِي هِيَ أَكْبَرُ مِنْ خَلْقِ النَّاسِ، أَفَلَيْسَ الَّذِي قَدَرَ عَلَى خَلْقِ هَذِهِ السَّمَوَاتِ، فِي ارْتِفَاعِهَا وَاتِّسَاعِهَا وَعَظَمَتِهَا وَمَا فِيهَا مِنَ الْكَوَاكِبِ الثَّوَابِتِ وَالسَّيَّارَاتِ، وَالْحَرَكَاتِ الْمُخْتَلِفَاتِ، وَالْآيَاتِ الْبَاهِرَاتِ، وَهَذِهِ الْأَرْضُ بِمَا فِيهَا مِنْ مِهَادٍ وَوِهَادٍ وَأَوْتَادٍ، وَبَرَارِي وَصَحَارِي وَقِفَارٍ، وَبِحَارٍ وَأَشْجَارٍ، وَنَبَاتٍ وَحَيَوَانٍ، عَلَى اخْتِلَافِ أَصْنَافِهَا وَمَنَافِعِهَا، وَأَشْكَالِهَا وَأَلْوَانِهَا؛ ﴿أَوَلَمْ يَرَوْا أَنَّ اللَّهَ الَّذِي خَلَقَ السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالأرْضَ وَلَمْ يَعْيَ بِخَلْقِهِنَّ بِقَادِرٍ عَلَى أَنْ يُحْيِيَ الْمَوْتَى بَلَى إِنَّهُ عَلَى كُلِّ شَيْءٍ قَدِيرٌ﴾ [الْأَحْقَافِ: ٣٣] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿أَوَلَمْ يَرَ الإنْسَانُ أَنَّا خَلَقْنَاهُ مِنْ نُطْفَةٍ فَإِذَا هُوَ خَصِيمٌ مُبِينٌ وَضَرَبَ لَنَا مَثَلا وَنَسِيَ خَلْقَهُ قَالَ مَنْ يُحْيِي الْعِظَامَ وَهِيَ رَمِيمٌ قُلْ يُحْيِيهَا الَّذِي أَنْشَأَهَا أَوَّلَ مَرَّةٍ وَهُوَ بِكُلِّ خَلْقٍ عَلِيمٌ الَّذِي جَعَلَ لَكُمْ مِنَ الشَّجَرِ الأخْضَرِ نَارًا فَإِذَا أَنْتُمْ مِنْهُ تُوقِدُونَ أَوَلَيْسَ الَّذِي خَلَقَ السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالأرْضَ بِقَادِرٍ عَلَى أَنْ يَخْلُقَ مِثْلَهُمْ بَلَى وَهُوَ الْخَلاقُ الْعَلِيمُ إِنَّمَا أَمْرُهُ إِذَا أَرَادَ شَيْئًا أَنْ يَقُولَ لَهُ كُنْ فَيَكُونُ فَسُبْحَانَ الَّذِي بِيَدِهِ مَلَكُوتُ كُلِّ شَيْءٍ وَإِلَيْهِ تُرْجَعُونَ﴾ [يس: ٧٧ -٨٣] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿إِنْ يَشَأْ يُذْهِبْكُمْ وَيَأْتِ بِخَلْقٍ جَدِيدٍ وَمَا ذَلِكَ عَلَى اللَّهِ بِعَزِيزٍ﴾ أَيْ: بِعَظِيمٍ وَلَا مُمْتَنِعٍ، بَلْ هُوَ سَهْلٌ عَلَيْهِ إِذَا خَالَفْتُمْ أَمْرَهُ، أَنْ يُذْهِبَكُمْ وَيَأْتِيَ بِآخَرِينَ عَلَى غَيْرِ صِفَتِكُمْ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿يَا أَيُّهَا النَّاسُ أَنْتُمُ الْفُقَرَاءُ إِلَى اللَّهِ وَاللَّهُ هُوَ الْغَنِيُّ الْحَمِيدُ إِنْ يَشَأْ يُذْهِبْكُمْ وَيَأْتِ بِخَلْقٍ جَدِيدٍ وَمَا ذَلِكَ عَلَى اللَّهِ بِعَزِيزٍ﴾ [فَاطِرٍ: ١٥ -١٧] ، وَقَالَ: ﴿وَإِنْ تَتَوَلَّوْا يَسْتَبْدِلْ قَوْمًا غَيْرَكُمْ ثُمَّ لَا يَكُونُوا أَمْثَالَكُمْ﴾ [مُحَمَّدٍ: ٣٨] ، وَقَالَ: ﴿يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا مَنْ يَرْتَدَّ مِنْكُمْ عَنْ دِينِهِ فَسَوْفَ يَأْتِي اللَّهُ بِقَوْمٍ يُحِبُّهُمْ وَيُحِبُّونَهُ﴾ [الْمَائِدَةِ: ٥٤] ، وَقَالَ: ﴿إِنْ يَشَأْ يُذْهِبْكُمْ أَيُّهَا النَّاسُ وَيَأْتِ بِآخَرِينَ وَكَانَ اللَّهُ عَلَى ذَلِكَ قَدِيرًا﴾ [النِّسَاءِ: ١٣٣] .

---

## 14:21 — verse 21

### Translation

He says: {And they will come forth [before Allah]}, that is, all created beings will come forth, the righteous among them and the wicked, before Allah alone, the One, the Overpowering. That is, they will be gathered before Him in an open expanse of the earth, which is a place with nothing in it to conceal anyone.

{Then the weak will say}, meaning the followers, to their leaders, their chiefs, and their great ones who had shown arrogance regarding the worship of Allah alone, having no partner, and regarding compliance with the messengers. They will say to them: {Indeed, we were followers of you}, meaning: whatever you commanded us, we obeyed and did, {so can you avert from us anything of the punishment of Allah?}, meaning: will you now ward off from us any part of Allah's punishment, as you used to promise us and make us hope for? The leaders will say to them: {If Allah had guided us, we would have guided you}, but the word of our Lord has come due against us, and the decree of Allah preceded concerning us and concerning you, and the word of punishment has become due upon the disbelievers.

{It is the same for us whether we show impatience or endure patiently; we have no escape}, meaning: there is no deliverance for us from what we are in, whether we bear it patiently or show impatience over it.

Abd al-Rahman ibn Zayd ibn Aslam said: the people of the Fire will say to one another: come, for the people of Paradise attained Paradise only through their weeping and their supplication to Allah, mighty and majestic is He. Come, let us weep and supplicate to Allah. So they will weep and supplicate, but when they see that this does not benefit them, they will say: come, for the people of Paradise attained Paradise only through patience. Come, let us be patient. So they will endure a patience the like of which has never been seen, but that will not benefit them either. At that point they will say: {It is the same for us whether we show impatience or endure patiently; we have no escape}.

I say: what is apparent is that this exchange takes place in the Fire, after they have entered it, as Allah, exalted is He, says: {And [mention] when they will dispute within the Fire, and the weak will say to those who had been arrogant, "Indeed, we were your followers, so can you avert from us a portion of the Fire?" Those who had been arrogant will say, "We are all in it together. Indeed, Allah has judged between the servants"} [Ghafir: 47, 48]. And Allah, exalted is He, says: {He will say, "Enter among nations who have passed on before you of jinn and mankind into the Fire." Every time a nation enters, it will curse its sister nation, until when they have all gathered therein, the last of them will say about the first of them, "Our Lord, these led us astray, so give them a double punishment of the Fire." He will say, "For each is a double, but you do not know." And the first of them will say to the last of them, "You had no advantage over us, so taste the punishment for what you used to earn"} [al-A'raf: 38, 39]. And Allah, exalted is He, says: {The Day their faces are turned about in the Fire, they will say, "Oh, would that we had obeyed Allah and obeyed the Messenger." And they will say, "Our Lord, indeed we obeyed our masters and our great ones, and they led us astray from the way. Our Lord, give them double the punishment and curse them with a great curse"} [al-Ahzab: 66-68].

As for their disputing with one another in the place of gathering, Allah, exalted is He, says: {And if you could but see when the wrongdoers are made to stand before their Lord, casting the blame on one another. Those who had been oppressed will say to those who had been arrogant, "If not for you, we would have been believers." Those who had been arrogant will say to those who had been oppressed, "Did we bar you from guidance after it had come to you? Rather, you were criminals." Those who had been oppressed will say to those who had been arrogant, "Rather, it was your plotting by night and day, when you commanded us to disbelieve in Allah and to set up rivals to Him." And they will confide their regret when they see the punishment. And We will put shackles on the necks of those who disbelieved. Will they be recompensed except for what they used to do?} [Saba: 31-33].

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ: ﴿وَبَرَزُوا [لِلَّهِ] ﴾ أَيْ: بَرَزَتِ الْخَلَائِقُ كُلُّهَا، بَرُّهَا وَفَاجِرُهَا لِلَّهِ وَحْدَهُ الْوَاحِدِ الْقَهَّارِ، أَيِ: اجْتَمَعُوا لَهُ فِي بِرَازٍ مِنَ الْأَرْضِ، وَهُوَ الْمَكَانُ الَّذِي لَيْسَ فِيهِ شَيْءٌ يَسْتُرُ أَحَدًا.

﴿فَقَالَ الضُّعَفَاءُ﴾ وَهْمُ الْأَتْبَاعُ لِقَادَتِهِمْ وَسَادَتِهِمْ وَكُبَرَائِهِمُ الَّذِينَ اسْتَكْبَرُوا عَنْ عِبَادَةِ.

اللَّهِ وَحْدَهُ لَا شَرِيكَ لَهُ، وَعَنْ مُوَافَقَةِ الرُّسُلِ، فَقَالُوا لَهُمْ: ﴿إِنَّا كُنَّا لَكُمْ تَبَعًا﴾ أَيْ: مَهْمَا أَمَرْتُمُونَا ائْتَمَرْنَا وَفَعَلْنَا، ﴿فَهَلْ أَنْتُمْ مُغْنُونَ عَنَّا مِنْ عَذَابِ اللَّهِ مِنْ شَيْءٍ﴾ أَيْ: فَهَلْ تَدْفَعُونَ عَنَّا شَيْئًا مِنْ عَذَابِ اللَّهِ، كَمَا كُنْتُمْ تَعِدُونَنَا وَتُمَنُّونَنَا؟ فَقَالَتِ الْقَادَةُ لَهُمْ: ﴿لَوْ هَدَانَا اللَّهُ لَهَدَيْنَاكُمْ﴾ وَلَكِنْ حَقَّ عَلَيْنَا قَوْلُ رَبِّنَا، وَسَبْقَ فِينَا وَفِيكُمْ قَدَرُ اللَّهِ، وَحَقَّتْ كَلِمَةُ الْعَذَابِ عَلَى الْكَافِرِينَ.

﴿سَوَاءٌ عَلَيْنَا أَجَزِعْنَا أَمْ صَبَرْنَا مَا لَنَا مِنْ مَحِيصٍ﴾ أَيْ: لَيْسَ لَنَا خَلاص مِمَّا نَحْنُ فِيهِ إِنْ صَبْرَنَا عَلَيْهِ أَوْ جَزِعْنَا مِنْهُ.

قَالَ عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ: إِنَّ أَهْلَ النَّارِ قَالَ بَعْضُهُمْ لِبَعْضٍ: تَعَالَوْا، فَإِنَّمَا أَدْرَكَ أَهْلُ الْجَنَّةِ الْجَنَّةَ بِبُكَائِهِمْ وَتَضَرُّعِهِمْ إِلَى اللَّهِ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، تَعَالَوْا نَبْكِ وَنَتَضَرَّعُ إِلَى اللَّهِ فَبَكَوْا وَتَضَرَّعُوا، فَلَّمَا رَأَوْا ذَلِكَ لَا يَنْفَعُهُمْ قَالُوا: تَعَالَوْا، فَإِنَّمَا أَدْرَكَ أَهْلُ الْجَنَّةِ الْجَنَّةَ بِالصَّبْرِ، تَعَالَوْا حَتَّى نَصْبِرَ فَصَبَرُوا صَبْرًا لَمْ يُرَ مِثْلُهُ، فَلَمْ يَنْفَعْهُمْ ذَلِكَ، فَعِنْدَ ذَلِكَ قَالُوا ﴿سَوَاءٌ عَلَيْنَا أَجَزِعْنَا أَمْ صَبَرْنَا مَا لَنَا مِنْ مَحِيصٍ﴾

قُلْتُ: وَالظَّاهِرُ أَنَّ هَذِهِ الْمُرَاجَعَةَ فِي النَّارِ بَعْدَ دُخُولِهِمْ إِلَيْهَا، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَإِذْ يَتَحَاجُّونَ فِي النَّارِ فَيَقُولُ الضُّعَفَاءُ لِلَّذِينَ اسْتَكْبَرُوا إِنَّا كُنَّا لَكُمْ تَبَعًا فَهَلْ أَنْتُمْ مُغْنُونَ عَنَّا نَصِيبًا مِنَ النَّارِ قَالَ الَّذِينَ اسْتَكْبَرُوا إِنَّا كُلٌّ فِيهَا إِنَّ اللَّهَ قَدْ حَكَمَ بَيْنَ الْعِبَادِ﴾ [غَافِرٍ: ٤٧، ٤٨] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿قَالَ ادْخُلُوا فِي أُمَمٍ قَدْ خَلَتْ مِنْ قَبْلِكُمْ مِنَ الْجِنِّ وَالإنْسِ فِي النَّارِ كُلَّمَا دَخَلَتْ أُمَّةٌ لَعَنَتْ أُخْتَهَا حَتَّى إِذَا ادَّارَكُوا فِيهَا جَمِيعًا قَالَتْ أُخْرَاهُمْ لأولاهُمْ رَبَّنَا هَؤُلاءِ أَضَلُّونَا فَآتِهِمْ عَذَابًا ضِعْفًا مِنَ النَّارِ قَالَ لِكُلٍّ ضِعْفٌ وَلَكِنْ لَا تَعْلَمُونَ وَقَالَتْ أُولاهُمْ لأخْرَاهُمْ فَمَا كَانَ لَكُمْ عَلَيْنَا مِنْ فَضْلٍ فَذُوقُوا الْعَذَابَ بِمَا كُنْتُمْ تَكْسِبُونَ﴾ [الأعراف: ٣٨، ٣٩] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿يَوْمَ تُقَلَّبُ وُجُوهُهُمْ فِي النَّارِ يَقُولُونَ يَا لَيْتَنَا أَطَعْنَا اللَّهَ وَأَطَعْنَا الرَّسُولا وَقَالُوا رَبَّنَا إِنَّا أَطَعْنَا سَادَتَنَا وَكُبَرَاءَنَا فَأَضَلُّونَا السَّبِيلا رَبَّنَا آتِهِمْ ضِعْفَيْنِ مِنَ الْعَذَابِ وَالْعَنْهُمْ لَعْنًا كَبِيرًا﴾ [الْأَحْزَابِ: ٦٦ -٦٨] .

وَأَمَّا تُخَاصِمُهُمْ فِي الْمَحْشَرِ، فَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلَوْ تَرَى إِذِ الظَّالِمُونَ مَوْقُوفُونَ عِنْدَ رَبِّهِمْ يَرْجِعُ بَعْضُهُمْ إِلَى بَعْضٍ الْقَوْلَ يَقُولُ الَّذِينَ اسْتُضْعِفُوا لِلَّذِينَ اسْتَكْبَرُوا لَوْلا أَنْتُمْ لَكُنَّا مُؤْمِنِينَ قَالَ الَّذِينَ اسْتَكْبَرُوا لِلَّذِينَ اسْتُضْعِفُوا أَنَحْنُ صَدَدْنَاكُمْ عَنِ الْهُدَى بَعْدَ إِذْ جَاءَكُمْ بَلْ كُنْتُمْ مُجْرِمِينَ وَقَالَ الَّذِينَ اسْتُضْعِفُوا لِلَّذِينَ اسْتَكْبَرُوا بَلْ مَكْرُ اللَّيْلِ وَالنَّهَارِ إِذْ تَأْمُرُونَنَا أَنْ نَكْفُرَ بِاللَّهِ وَنَجْعَلَ لَهُ أَنْدَادًا وَأَسَرُّوا النَّدَامَةَ لَمَّا رَأَوُا الْعَذَابَ وَجَعَلْنَا الأغْلالَ فِي أَعْنَاقِ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا هَلْ يُجْزَوْنَ إِلا مَا كَانُوا يَعْمَلُونَ﴾ [سَبَأٍ: ٣١ -٣٣] .

---

## 14:22-23 — verses 22-23 (shared commentary)

### Translation

God Most High informs us of the sermon which Iblis [may God curse him] delivered to his followers, after God had judged between His servants, admitting the believers into the gardens and settling the disbelievers in the lowest depths. Iblis, may God curse him, then stood up among them as an orator, in order to add sorrow to their sorrow, loss to their loss, and regret to their regret. He said: {Indeed, God promised you a true promise}, that is, through the tongues of His messengers, and He promised you, in following them, deliverance and safety, and it was a true promise and a truthful report. "As for me, I promised you and I broke my promise to you," as God Most High said: {He promises them and gives them false hopes, but Satan promises them nothing except delusion} [al-Nisa: 120].

Then he said: {And I had no authority over you}, meaning: I had no proof or argument over you in what I called you to, establishing the truth of what I promised you, {except that I called you and you responded to me}, by that alone. This is despite the fact that the messengers had established against you sound proofs and evidences of the truth of what they brought you, yet you opposed them and thus came to be in the state you are now in. {So do not blame me} today, {but blame yourselves}, for the fault is yours, since you opposed the proofs and followed me merely because I called you to falsehood. {I cannot help you}, meaning: I cannot benefit you, rescue you, or deliver you from what you are in, {nor can you help me}, meaning: nor can you benefit me by rescuing me from the punishment and retribution I am in. {Indeed, I disbelieved in your associating me [with God] before}.

Qatadah said: that is, because of your associating me [with God] before.

Ibn Jarir said: he means, I have denied being a partner to God, Mighty and Majestic.

What Ibn Jarir said is the stronger view, as God Most High said: {And who is more astray than one who calls upon, besides God, those who will not answer him until the Day of Resurrection, and who are unaware of their calls upon them? And when mankind is gathered, they will be enemies to them and will deny their worship} [al-Ahqaf: 5-6], and He said: {No! They will deny their worship and will be opponents against them} [Maryam: 82].

His saying: {Indeed the wrongdoers}, that is, in their turning away from the truth and following falsehood, {will have a painful punishment}.

What is apparent from the context of the verse is that this sermon of Iblis takes place after they have entered the Fire, as we mentioned previously. However, there has come in a hadith narrated by Ibn Abi Hatim, and this is his wording, and by Ibn Jarir, from the narration of Abd al-Rahman ibn Ziyad: Dukhayn al-Hajri told me, from Uqbah ibn Amir, from the Messenger of God ﷺ, that he said: "When God gathers the first and the last generations and judges between them, and finishes the judgment, the believers say: 'Our Lord has judged between us, so who will intercede for us?' They say: 'Let us go to Adam,' and he mentioned Noah, Abraham, Moses, and Jesus (peace be upon them), and Jesus says: 'I will direct you to the unlettered Prophet.' So they come to me, and God permits me to stand before Him, and there rises from my place the sweetest fragrance anyone has ever smelled, until I come to my Lord and He grants me the power of intercession, and He places upon me a light from the hair of my head to the nail of my foot. Then the disbelievers say: 'The believers have found someone to intercede for them, so who will intercede for us? It was none other than Iblis who led us astray.' So they come to Iblis and say: 'The believers have found someone to intercede for them, so stand and intercede for us, for it was you who led us astray.' So he stands, and there rises from his place the foulest stench anyone has ever smelled, and then their wailing grows greater. {And Satan will say, when the matter has been decided: Indeed, God promised you a true promise, and I promised you but broke my promise to you. I had no authority over you except that I called you and you responded to me, so do not blame me but blame yourselves}."

This is the wording of Ibn Abi Hatim. It was also narrated by Ibn al-Mubarak, from Rishdin ibn Sa'd, from Abd al-Rahman ibn Ziyad ibn An'um, from Dukhayn, from Uqbah, raised to the Prophet ﷺ (marfu').

Muhammad ibn Ka'b al-Qurazi, may God have mercy on him, said: When the people of the Fire say: {It is the same for us whether we show impatience or bear patiently; we have no place of escape}, Iblis says to them: {Indeed, God promised you a true promise} the verse. When they hear his statement, they hate themselves, and it is called out to them: {The hatred of God is greater than your hatred of yourselves, when you were called to faith and you disbelieved} [Ghafir: 10].

Amir al-Sha'bi said: two orators will stand on the Day of Resurrection above the heads of the people. God will say to Jesus, son of Mary (peace be upon him): {Did you say to the people, "Take me and my mother as two gods besides God"?} up to His saying: {God will say: This is the Day when the truthful will benefit from their truthfulness} [al-Ma'idah: 116, 119].
