وَقَالَ تَعَالَى رَادًّا عَلَيْهِمْ فِي قَوْلِهِمْ هَذَا: ﴿أَوَلَمْ تَكُونُوا أَقْسَمْتُمْ مِنْ قَبْلُ مَا لَكُمْ مِنْ زَوَالٍ﴾ أي: أو لم تَكُونُوا تَحْلِفُونَ مِنْ قَبْلِ هَذِهِ الْحَالِ: أَنَّهُ لَا زَوَالَ لَكُمْ عَمَّا أَنْتُمْ فِيهِ، وَأَنَّهُ لَا مَعَادَ وَلَا جَزَاءَ، فَذُوقُوا هَذَا بِذَاكَ.

قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ وَغَيْرُهُ: ﴿مَا لَكُمْ مِنْ زَوَالٍ﴾ أَيْ: مَا لَكَمْ مِنِ انْتِقَالٍ مِنَ الدُّنْيَا إِلَى الْآخِرَةِ، كَمَا أَخْبَرَ عَنْهُمْ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَأَقْسَمُوا بِاللَّهِ جَهْدَ أَيْمَانِهِمْ لَا يَبْعَثُ اللَّهُ مَنْ يَمُوتُ بَلَى وَعْدًا عَلَيْهِ حَقًّا﴾ [النَّحْلِ: ٣٨] .

﴿وَسَكَنْتُمْ فِي مَسَاكِنِ الَّذِينَ ظَلَمُوا أَنْفُسَهُمْ وَتَبَيَّنَ لَكُمْ كَيْفَ فَعَلْنَا بِهِمْ وَضَرَبْنَا لَكُمُ الأمْثَالَ﴾ أَيْ: قَدْ رَأَيْتُمْ وَبَلَغَكُمْ مَا أَحْلَلْنَا بِالْأُمَمِ الْمُكَذِّبَةِ قَبْلَكُمْ، وَمَعَ هَذَا لَمْ يَكُنْ لَكُمْ فِيهِمْ مُعْتَبَرٌ، وَلَمْ يَكُنْ فِيمَا أَوْقَعْنَا بِهِمْ مُزْدَجَرٌ لَكُمْ ﴿حِكْمَةٌ بَالِغَةٌ فَمَا تُغْنِ النُّذُرُ﴾ [الْقَمَرِ: ٥] .

وَقَدْ رَوَى شُعْبَةُ، عَنْ أَبِي إِسْحَاقَ، عَنْ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ [بْنِ دَابِيلَ] أَنَّ عَلِيًّا، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ فِي هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ: ﴿وَإِنْ كَانَ مَكْرُهُمْ لِتَزُولَ مِنْهُ الْجِبَالُ﴾ قَالَ: أَخَذَ ذَاكَ الَّذِي حَاجَّ إِبْرَاهِيمُ فِي رَبِّهِ نَسْرَيْنِ صَغِيرَيْنِ، فَرَبَّاهُمَا حَتَّى اسْتَغْلَظَا وَاسْتَعْلَجَا وَشَبَّا .

قَالَ: فَأَوْثَقَ رِجْل كُلِّ وَاحِدٍ مِنْهُمَا بِوَتَدٍ إِلَى تَابُوتٍ، وَجَوَّعَهُمَا، وَقَعَدَ هُوَ وَرَجُلٌ آخَرُ فِي التَّابُوتِ قَالَ:-وَرَفَعَ فِي التَّابُوتِ عَصًا عَلَى رَأْسِهِ اللَّحْمُ -قَالَ: فَطَارَا [قَالَ] وَجَعَلَ يَقُولُ لِصَاحِبِهِ: انْظُرْ، مَا تَرَى؟ قَالَ: أَرَى كَذَا وَكَذَا، حَتَّى قَالَ: أَرَى الدُّنْيَا كُلَّهَا كَأَنَّهَا ذباب. قال: فقال: صوب العصا، فَصَوَّبَهَا، فَهَبَطَا. قَالَ: فَهُوَ قَوْلُ اللَّهِ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ: "وَإِنْ كَادَ مَكْرُهُمْ لِتَزُولَ مِنْهُ الْجِبَالُ". قَالَ أَبُو إِسْحَاقَ: وَكَذَلِكَ هِيَ فِي قِرَاءَةِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ: "وَإِنْ كَادَ مَكْرُهُمْ" .

قُلْتُ: وَكَذَا رُوي عَنْ أُبَيِّ بْنِ كَعْبٍ، وَعُمَرَ بْنِ الْخَطَّابِ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمَا، أَنَّهُمَا قَرَآ: "وَإِنْ كَادَ"، كَمَا قَرَأَ عَلِيٌّ. وَكَذَا رَوَاهُ سُفْيَانُ الثَّوْرِيُّ، وَإِسْرَائِيلُ، عَنْ أَبِي إِسْحَاقَ، عَنْ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنِ أُذُنَانَ عَنْ عَلِيٍّ، فَذَكَرَ نَحْوَهُ.

وَكَذَا رُوي عَنْ عِكْرِمَةَ أَنَّ سِيَاقَ هَذِهِ الْقِصَّةِ لِنَمْرُودَ مَلِكِ كَنْعَانَ: أَنَّهُ رَامَ أَسْبَابَ السَّمَاءِ بِهَذِهِ الْحِيلَةِ وَالْمَكْرِ، كَمَا رَامَ ذَلِكَ بَعْدَهُ فِرْعَوْنُ مَلِكُ الْقِبْطِ فِي بِنَاءِ الصَّرْحِ، فَعَجَزَا وَضَعُفَا. وَهُمَا أَقَلُّ وَأَحْقَرُ، وَأَصْغَرُ وَأَدْحَرُ.

وَذَكَرَ مُجَاهِدٌ هَذِهِ الْقِصَّةَ عَنْ بُخْتُنَصَّرَ، وَأَنَّهُ لَمَّا انْقَطَعَ بَصَرُهُ عَنِ الْأَرْضِ وَأَهْلِهَا، نُودِيَ أَيُّهَا الطَّاغِيَةُ: أَيْنَ تُرِيدُ؟ فَفَرق، ثُمَّ سَمِعَ الصَّوْتَ فَوْقَهُ فَصَوَّبَ الرِّمَاحَ، فصَوبت النُّسُورُ، فَفَزِعَتِ الْجِبَالُ مِنْ هَدَّتِهَا، وَكَادَتِ الْجِبَالُ أَنْ تَزُولَ مِنْ حِسِّ ذَلِكَ، فَذَلِكَ قَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَإِنْ كَانَ مَكْرُهُمْ لِتَزُولَ مِنْهُ الْجِبَالُ﴾

وَنَقَلَ ابْنُ جُريج عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ أَنَّهُ قَرَأَهَا: "لَتَزُولُ مِنْهُ الْجِبَالُ"، بِفَتْحِ اللَّامِ الْأُولَى، وَضَمِّ الثَّانِيَةِ.

وَرَوَى الْعَوْفِيُّ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَإِنْ كَانَ مَكْرُهُمْ لِتَزُولَ مِنْهُ الْجِبَالُ﴾ يَقُولُ: مَا كَانَ مَكْرُهُمْ لِتَزُولَ مِنْهُ الْجِبَالُ. وَكَذَا قَالَ الْحَسَنُ الْبَصْرِيُّ، وَوَجَّهَهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ بِأَنَّ هَذَا الَّذِي فَعَلُوهُ بِأَنْفُسِهِمْ مِنْ كُفْرِهِمْ بِاللَّهِ وَشِرْكِهِمْ بِهِ، مَا ضَرَّ ذَلِكَ شَيْئًا مِنَ الْجِبَالِ وَلَا غَيْرِهَا، وَإِنَّمَا عَادَ وَبَالُ ذَلِكَ عَلَى أَنْفُسِهِمْ.

قُلْتُ: وَيُشْبِهُ هَذَا إِذًا قَوْلَهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلا تَمْشِ فِي الأرْضِ مَرَحًا إِنَّكَ لَنْ تَخْرِقَ الأرْضَ وَلَنْ تَبْلُغَ الْجِبَالَ طُولا﴾ [الْإِسْرَاءِ: ٣٧] .

وَالْقَوْلُ الثَّانِي فِي تَفْسِيرِهَا: مَا رَوَاهُ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿وَإِنْ كَانَ مَكْرُهُمْ لِتَزُولَ مِنْهُ الْجِبَالُ﴾ يَقُولُ شِرْكُهُمْ، كَقَوْلِهِ: ﴿تَكَادُ السَّمَاوَاتُ يَتَفَطَّرْنَ مِنْهُ وَتَنْشَقُّ الأرْضُ وَتَخِرُّ الْجِبَالُ هَدّاً أَنْ دَعَوْا لِلرَّحْمَنِ وَلَدًا﴾ [مَرْيَمَ: ٩٠ -٩١] ، وهكذا قال الضحاك وقتادة.

---

## 14:47-48 — verses 47-48 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says, affirming His promise and confirming it: {So do not think that Allah is one who breaks His promise to His messengers} meaning: of granting them victory in the life of this world and on the Day when the witnesses will stand.

Then He informs that He possesses might, such that nothing He wills can be withheld from Him, nor can He be overcome, and that He possesses vengeance against whoever disbelieves in Him and denies Him: {Woe that Day to the deniers} [al-Tur: 11]. It is for this reason that He said: {On the Day when the earth will be changed into another earth, and the heavens} meaning: this promise of His shall come to pass on the Day when the earth is changed into another earth, one unlike this familiar, known form, as has come in the two Sahihs, from the hadith of Abu Hazim, from Sahl ibn Sa'd, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said, "The people will be gathered on the Day of Resurrection upon an earth that is white and reddish-brown, like a loaf of fine flour, with no landmark for anyone upon it."

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Muhammad ibn Abi Adi, from Dawud, from al-Sha'bi, from Masruq, from A'isha, that she said: I was the first of the people to ask the Messenger of Allah ﷺ about this verse: {On the Day when the earth will be changed into another earth, and the heavens, and they will come forth before Allah, the One, the Subduer of all}. She said: I said, "Where will the people be on that Day, O Messenger of Allah?" He said, "Upon the Bridge (al-Sirat)."

Muslim related it alone without al-Bukhari, and al-Tirmidhi and Ibn Majah related it from the hadith of Dawud ibn Abi Hind, through the same chain, and al-Tirmidhi said: hasan sahih (sound and authentic).

Ahmad also related it, from Affan, from Wuhayb, from Dawud, from al-Sha'bi, from her, without mentioning Masruq.

Qatada said, from Hassan ibn Bilal al-Muzani, from A'isha, may Allah be pleased with her, that she asked the Messenger of Allah ﷺ about Allah's saying: {On the Day when the earth will be changed into another earth, and the heavens}. He said, and she said, "O Messenger of Allah, where will the people be on that Day?" He said, "You have asked me about something that no one from my nation has ever asked me. That is, the people will be upon the bridge over Hell."

Imam Ahmad related, from the hadith of Habib ibn Abi Amra, from Mujahid, from Ibn Abbas: A'isha told me that she asked the Messenger of Allah ﷺ about His saying, the Almighty: {And the earth entirely will be in His grip on the Day of Resurrection, and the heavens will be folded in His right hand} [al-Zumar: 67]. "So where will the people be on that Day, O Messenger of Allah?" He said, "They will be upon the back of Hell."

Ibn Jarir said: [chain] al-Hasan, [chain] Ali ibn al-Ja'd, [chain] al-Qasim, who heard al-Hasan say: A'isha said, "O Messenger of Allah, {On the Day when the earth will be changed into another earth}, so where will the people be on that Day?" He said, "This is something no one has ever asked me." He said, "Upon the Bridge, O A'isha."

Ahmad also related it, from Affan, from al-Qasim ibn al-Fadl, from al-Hasan, through the same chain.

Imam Muslim ibn al-Hajjaj said in his Sahih: [chain] al-Hasan ibn Ali al-Hulwani, [chain] Abu Tawba al-Rabi' ibn Nafi', [chain] Mu'awiya ibn Sallam, from Zayd (his brother), that he heard Abu Sallam, [chain] Abu Asma' al-Rahabi, that Thawban, the freed slave of the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, told him: I was standing near the Messenger of Allah ﷺ when a rabbi from among the rabbis of the Jews came to him and said, "Peace be upon you, O Muhammad." I pushed him a push that nearly knocked him down, and he said, "Why do you push me?" I said, "Will you not say, 'O Messenger of Allah'?" The Jew said, "We only call him by the name his family named him." The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said, "Indeed my name is Muhammad, the name my family gave me." The Jew said, "I have come to ask you." The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said, "Will it benefit you if I tell you?" He said, "I am listening with my ears." So the Messenger of Allah ﷺ scratched with a stick he had, and said, "Ask." The Jew said, "Where will the people be on the Day when the earth is changed into another earth, and the heavens?" The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said, "They will be in the darkness, before the bridge." He said, "Then who will be the first of the people to cross?" He said, "The poor among the emigrants (Muhajirin)." The Jew said, "And what will be their gift when they enter Paradise?" He said, "The extra lobe of the liver of the great fish." He said, "And what will they eat after that?" He said, "The bull of Paradise, which used to graze on its edges, will be slaughtered for them." He said, "And what will they drink with it?" He said, "From a spring there called Salsabil." He said, "You have spoken truly." He said, "And I have come to ask you about something that no one on earth knows except a prophet, or one man or two men." He said, "Will it benefit you if I tell you?" He said, "I am listening with my ears." He said, "I have come to ask you about the child." He said, "The man's fluid is white and the woman's fluid is yellow. When they meet, if the man's semen prevails over the woman's semen, the child is male, by Allah's permission, the Almighty, and if the woman's semen prevails over the man's semen, the child is female, by Allah's permission." The Jew said, "You have spoken truly, and indeed you are a prophet." Then he departed, and the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said, "This man has asked me about matters concerning which I had no knowledge at all, until Allah brought it to me."

Abu Ja'far ibn Jarir al-Tabari said: [chain] Ibn Awf, [chain] Abu al-Mughira, [chain] Ibn Abi Maryam, [chain] Sa'id ibn Thawban al-Kala'i, from Abu Ayyub al-Ansari, who said: A rabbi from the Jews came to the Prophet ﷺ and said, "Tell me, when Allah says in His Book: {On the Day when the earth will be changed into another earth, and the heavens}, where will creation be at that time?" He said, "They will be the guests of Allah, and nothing He possesses will fail to suffice them."

Ibn Abi Hatim related it, from the hadith of Abu Bakr ibn Abd Allah ibn Abi Maryam, through the same chain.

Shu'ba said: [chain] Abu Ishaq, who heard Amr ibn Maymun, and sometimes he would say "Abd Allah said," and sometimes he would not say it, so I said to him, "From Abd Allah?" And he said: I heard Amr ibn Maymun say, regarding {On the Day when the earth will be changed into another earth}: an earth like white silver, pure, upon which no blood has been spilled and upon which no sin has been committed, where sight will reach to its farthest limit and the caller's voice will be heard by all, barefoot and naked as they were created. He said: I think he said: standing, until the sweat reaches up to their mouths.

It was also related through another route, from Shu'ba, from Isra'il, from Abu Ishaq, from Amr ibn Maymun, from Ibn Mas'ud, similarly. Asim likewise related it, from Zirr, from Ibn Mas'ud, through the same chain.

Sufyan al-Thawri said, from Abu Ishaq, from Amr ibn Maymun, that he did not attribute it to anyone further. Ibn Jarir cited all of this.

The hafiz Abu Bakr al-Bazzar said: [chain] Muhammad ibn Abd Allah ibn Ubayd ibn Aqil, [chain] Sahl ibn Hammad Abu Attab, [chain] Jarir ibn Ayyub, from Abu Ishaq, from Amr ibn Maymun, from Abd Allah, from the Prophet ﷺ, regarding the saying of Allah, mighty and majestic: {On the Day when the earth will be changed into another earth}, he said: "A white earth upon which no blood has fallen and upon which no sin has been committed." Then he said: We do not know of anyone who traced it back as a raised report (marfu') except Jarir ibn Ayyub, and he is not strong (as a narrator).

Then Ibn Jarir said: [chain] Abu Kurayb, [chain] Mu'awiya ibn Hisham, from Sinan, from Jabir al-Ju'fi, from Abu Jubayra, from Zayd, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ sent for the Jews and said, "Do you know why I have sent for them?" They said, "Allah and His Messenger know best." He said, "I sent for them to ask them about Allah's saying: {On the Day when the earth will be changed into another earth}, that it will be, on that Day, white like silver." So when they came, he asked them, and they said, "It will be white like fine flour."

Similarly it was related from Ali, Ibn Abbas, Anas ibn Malik, and Mujahid ibn Jabr, that it will be changed on the Day of Resurrection into an earth of silver.

It is related from Ali, may Allah be pleased with him, that he said: The earth will become silver, and the heavens gold.

Al-Rabi' said, from Abu al-Aliya, from Ubayy ibn Ka'b, who said: The heavens will become gardens.

Abu Mi'shar said, from Muhammad ibn Ka'b al-Qurazi, or from Muhammad ibn Qays, regarding His saying: {On the Day when the earth will be changed into another earth}, he said: it will be changed into a loaf of bread from which the believers will eat, from beneath their feet.

Waki' likewise related, from Umar ibn Bashir al-Hamdani, from Sa'id ibn Jubayr, regarding His saying: {On the Day when the earth will be changed into another earth}, he said: it will be changed into white bread, and the believer will eat from beneath his feet.

Al-A'mash said, from Khaythama, who said: Abd Allah, that is Ibn Mas'ud, said: The whole earth on the Day of Resurrection will be fire, and Paradise will be behind it, and they will see its full-breasted maidens and its drinking-vessels, and the sweat will reach up to people's mouths, or the sweat will reach that level among them, while they have not yet reached the reckoning (al-hisab).

Al-A'mash also said, from al-Minhal ibn Amr, from Qays ibn al-Sakan, who said: Abd Allah said: The whole earth will be fire on the Day of Resurrection, and Paradise will be behind it, and they will see its drinking-vessels and its full-breasted maidens. By the One in whose hand is the soul of Abd Allah, a man will pour forth sweat until his foot sinks into the ground, then it will rise until it reaches his nose, and yet the reckoning will not have touched him. They said, "Why is that, O Abu Abd al-Rahman?" He said, "Because of what he sees the people encountering."

Abu Ja'far al-Razi said, from al-Rabi' ibn Anas, from Ka'b, regarding His saying: {On the Day when the earth will be changed into another earth, and the heavens}, he said: The heavens will become gardens, and the place of the sea will become fire, and the earth will be changed into another.

In the hadith related by Abu Dawud: "No one should sail upon the sea except one going out for jihad, or for pilgrimage (hajj), or for the lesser pilgrimage (umra), for beneath the sea there is fire, or: beneath the fire there is a sea."

And in the well-known hadith of the Trumpet (al-Sur), related from Abu Hurayra, from the Prophet ﷺ, that he said: "The earth will be changed into another earth, and the heavens likewise, and He will spread it out and stretch it like the stretching of Ukazi leather, so that you will see in it no crookedness and no unevenness. Then Allah will drive the creation with a single drive, and behold, they will be upon this changed earth."

His saying: {and they will come forth before Allah} means: all created beings will come out of their graves, before Allah, {the One, the Subduer of all} meaning: He who has subdued everything and overcome it, before whom all necks bow in submission, and before whom all minds are humbled.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُقَرِّرًا لِوَعْدِهِ وَمُؤَكِّدًا: ﴿فَلا تَحْسَبَنَّ اللَّهَ مُخْلِفَ وَعْدِهِ رُسُلَهُ﴾ أَيْ: مِنْ نُصْرَتِهِمْ فِي الْحَيَاةِ الدُّنْيَا وَيَوْمَ يَقُومُ الْأَشْهَادُ.

ثُمَّ أَخْبَرَ أَنَّهُ ذُو عِزَّةٍ لَا يَمْتَنِعُ عَلَيْهِ شَيْءٌ أَرَادَهُ، وَلَا يُغَالَبُ، وَذُو انْتِقَامٍ مِمَّنْ كَفَرَ بِهِ وَجَحَدَهُ ﴿وَيْلٌ يَوْمَئِذٍ لِلْمُكَذِّبِينَ﴾ [الطُّورِ: ١١] ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿يَوْمَ تُبَدَّلُ الأرْضُ غَيْرَ الأرْضِ وَالسَّمَاوَاتُ﴾ أَيْ: وَعْدُهُ هَذَا حَاصِلٌ يَوْمَ تُبَدَّلُ الْأَرْضُ غَيْرَ الْأَرْضِ، وَهِيَ هَذِهِ عَلَى غَيْرِ الصِّفَةِ الْمَأْلُوفَةِ الْمَعْرُوفَةِ، كَمَا جَاءَ فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ أَبِي حَازِمٍ، عَنْ سَهْلِ بْنِ سَعْدٍ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "يُحْشَرُ النَّاسُ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ عَلَى أَرْضٍ بَيْضَاءَ عَفْرَاءَ، كَقُرْصَةِ النَّقِيِّ، لَيْسَ فِيهَا مَعْلَمٌ لِأَحَدٍ" .

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ أَبِي عَدِيٍّ، عَنْ دَاوُدَ، عَنِ الشَّعْبِيِّ، عَنْ مَسْرُوقٍ، عَنْ عَائِشَةَ أَنَّهَا قَالَتْ: أَنَا أَوَّلُ النَّاسِ سَأَلَ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ عَنْ هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ: ﴿يَوْمَ تُبَدَّلُ الأرْضُ غَيْرَ الأرْضِ وَالسَّمَاوَاتُ وَبَرَزُوا لِلَّهِ الْوَاحِدِ الْقَهَّارِ﴾ قَالَتْ: قُلْتُ: أَيْنَ النَّاسُ يَوْمَئِذٍ يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ؟ قَالَ: "عَلَى الصِّرَاطِ".

رَوَاهُ مُسْلِمٌ مُنْفَرِدًا بِهِ دُونَ الْبُخَارِيِّ، وَالتِّرْمِذِيِّ، وَابْنِ مَاجَهْ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ دَاوُدَ بْنِ أَبِي هِنْدٍ، بِهِ وَقَالَ التِّرْمِذِيُّ: حَسَنٌ صَحِيحٌ.

وَرَوَاهُ أَحْمَدُ أَيْضًا، عَنْ عَفَّانَ، عَنْ وُهَيْبٍ عَنْ دَاوُدَ، عَنِ الشَّعْبِيِّ، عَنْهَا وَلَمْ يَذْكُرْ مَسْرُوقًا .

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ، عَنْ حَسَّانَ بْنِ بِلَالٍ الْمُزَنِيِّ، عَنْ عَائِشَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهَا، أَنَّهَا سَأَلَتْ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ عَنْ قَوْلِ اللَّهُ: ﴿يَوْمَ تُبَدَّلُ الأرْضُ غَيْرَ الأرْضِ وَالسَّمَاوَاتُ﴾ قَالَ: قَالَتْ يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، فَأَيْنَ النَّاسُ يَوْمَئِذٍ؟ قَالَ: "لَقَدْ سَأَلْتِنِي عَنْ شَيْءٍ مَا سَأَلَنِي عَنْهُ أَحَدٌ مِنْ أُمَّتِي، ذَاكَ أَنَّ النَّاسَ عَلَى جِسْرِ جَهَنَّمَ .

وَرَوَى الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ حَبِيبِ بْنِ أَبِي عَمْرَةَ، عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، حَدَّثَتْنِي عَائِشَةَ أَنَّهَا سَأَلَتْ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ، عن قَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَالأرْضُ جَمِيعًا قَبْضَتُهُ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ وَالسَّماوَاتُ مَطْوِيَّاتٌ بِيَمِينِهِ﴾ [الزمر: ٦٧] ، فَأَيْنَ النَّاسُ يَوْمَئِذٍ يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ؟ قَالَ: "هُمْ عَلَى مَتْنِ جَهَنَّمَ" .

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنَا الْحَسَنُ، حَدَّثَنَا عَلِيُّ بْنُ الْجَعْدِ، أَخْبَرَنِي الْقَاسِمُ، سَمِعْتُ الْحَسَنَ قَالَ: قَالَتْ عَائِشَةُ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، ﴿يَوْمَ تُبَدَّلُ الأرْضُ غَيْرَ الأرْضِ﴾ فَأَيْنَ النَّاسُ يَوْمَئِذٍ؟ قَالَ: "إِنَّ هَذَا شَيْءٌ مَا سَأَلَنِي عَنْهُ أَحَدٌ"، قَالَ: "عَلَى الصِّرَاطِ يَا عَائِشَةُ".

وَرَوَاهُ أَحْمَدُ، عَنْ عَفَّانَ عَنِ الْقَاسِمِ بْنِ الْفَضْلِ، عَنِ الْحَسَنِ، بِهِ .

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ مُسْلِمُ بْنُ الْحَجَّاجِ فِي صَحِيحِهِ: حَدَّثَنِي الْحَسَنُ بْنُ عَلِيٍّ الْحُلْوَانِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو تَوْبة الرَّبِيعُ بْنُ نَافِعٍ، حَدَّثَنَا مُعَاوِيَةُ بْنُ سَلَّامٍ، عَنْ زَيْدٍ -يَعْنِي: أَخَاهُ -أَنَّهُ سَمِعَ أَبَا سَلَّامٍ، حَدَّثَنِي أَبُو أَسْمَاءَ الرَّحَبِي؛ أَنَّ ثَوْبَانَ مَوْلَى رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ حَدَّثَهُ قَالَ: كُنْتُ قَائِمًا عِنْدَ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ، فَجَاءَهُ حَبر مِنْ أَحْبَارِ الْيَهُودِ، فَقَالَ: السَّلَامُ عَلَيْكَ يَا مُحَمَّدُ. فَدَفَعْتُهُ دَفْعَةً كَادَ يُصرَع مِنْهَا، فَقَالَ: لِمَ تَدْفَعُنِي؟ فَقُلْتُ: أَلَا تَقُولُ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ؟! فَقَالَ الْيَهُودِيُّ: إِنَّمَا نَدْعُوهُ بِاسْمِهِ الَّذِي سَمّاه بِهِ أَهْلُهُ! فَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "إِنَّ اسْمِي مُحَمَّدٌ الَّذِي سَمَّانِي بِهِ أَهْلِي". فَقَالَ الْيَهُودِيُّ: جِئْتُ أَسْأَلُكَ. فَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "أَيَنْفَعُكَ شَيْءٌ إِنْ حَدَّثْتُكَ؟ " فَقَالَ: أَسْمَعُ بِأُذُنَيَّ. فَنَكَتَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ بِعُودٍ مَعَهُ، فَقَالَ: "سَلْ". فَقَالَ الْيَهُودِيُّ: أَيْنَ يَكُونُ النَّاسُ يَوْمَ تُبَدَّلُ الْأَرْضُ غَيْرَ الْأَرْضِ وَالسَّمَوَاتُ؟ فَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "هُمْ فِي الظُّلْمَةِ دُونَ الْجِسْرِ" قَالَ: فَمَنْ أَوَّلُ النَّاسِ إِجَازَةً؟ قَالَ: فَقَالَ: " [فُقَرَاءُ] الْمُهَاجِرِينَ". قَالَ الْيَهُودِيُّ: فَمَا تُحْفَتهُم حِينَ يَدْخُلُونَ الْجَنَّةَ؟ قَالَ: "زِيَادَةُ كَبِدِ النُّونِ" قَالَ: فَمَا غِذَاؤُهُمْ فِي أَثَرِهَا؟ قَالَ: "يُنْحَرُ لَهُمْ ثَوْرُ الْجَنَّةِ الَّذِي كَانَ يَأْكُلُ مِنْ أَطْرَافِهَا". قَالَ: فَمَا شَرَابُهُمْ عَلَيْهِ؟ قَالَ: "مِنْ عَيْنٍ فِيهَا تُسَمَّى سَلْسَبِيلًا". قَالَ: صَدَقْتَ. قَالَ: وَجِئْتُ أَسْأَلُكَ عَنْ شَيْءٍ لَا يَعْلَمُهُ أَحَدٌ مِنْ أَهْلِ الْأَرْضِ إِلَّا نَبِيٌّ أَوْ رَجُلٌ أَوْ رَجُلَانِ؟ قَالَ: "أَيَنْفَعُكَ إِنْ حَدَّثْتُكَ؟ " قَالَ: أَسْمَعُ بِأُذُنَيَّ. قَالَ: جِئْتُ أَسْأَلُكَ عَنِ الْوَلَدِ. قَالَ: "مَاءُ الرَّجُلِ أَبْيَضُ وَمَاءُ الْمَرْأَةِ أَصْفَرُ، فَإِذَا اجْتَمَعَا فَعَلا منيُّ الرَّجُلِ منيَّ الْمَرْأَةِ أَذْكَرَا بِإِذْنِ اللَّهِ -تعالى -وَإِذَا عَلَا مَنِيُّ الْمَرْأَةِ مَنِيَّ الرَّجُلِ أنَّثا بِإِذْنِ اللَّهِ" قَالَ الْيَهُودِيُّ: لَقَدْ صَدَقْتَ، وَإِنَّكَ لَنَبِيٌّ. ثُمَّ انْصَرَفَ، فَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "لَقَدْ سَأَلَنِي هَذَا عَنِ الَّذِي سَأَلَنِي عَنْهُ، وَمَا لِي عِلْمٌ بِشَيْءٍ مِنْهُ، حَتَّى أَتَانِيَ اللَّهُ بِهِ" .

[وَ] قَالَ أَبُو جَعْفَرٍ بْنُ جَرِيرٍ الطَّبَرِيُّ: حَدَّثَنِي ابْنُ عَوْفٍ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو الْمُغِيرَةِ، حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ أَبِي مَرْيَمَ، حَدَّثَنَا سَعِيدُ بْنُ ثَوْبَانَ الكَلاعي، عَنْ أَبِي أَيُّوبَ الْأَنْصَارِيِّ، قَالَ: أَتَى النبيَّ ﷺ حَبْر مِنَ الْيَهُودِ فَقَالَ: أَرَأَيْتَ إِذْ يَقُولُ اللَّهُ فِي كِتَابِهِ: ﴿يَوْمَ تُبَدَّلُ الأرْضُ غَيْرَ الأرْضِ وَالسَّمَاوَاتُ﴾ فَأَيْنَ الخَلْق عِنْدَ ذَلِكَ؟ فَقَالَ: "أَضْيَافُ اللَّهِ، فَلَنْ يُعْجِزَهُمْ مَا لَدَيْهِ" .

وَرَوَاهُ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ أَبِي بَكْرِ بْنِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ أَبِي مَرْيَمَ، بِهِ.

وَقَالَ شُعْبَةُ: أَخْبَرَنَا أَبُو إِسْحَاقَ، سَمِعْتُ عَمْرَو بْنَ مَيْمُونٍ -وَرُبَّمَا قَالَ: قَالَ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ، وَرُبَّمَا لَمْ يَقُلْ -فَقُلْتُ لَهُ: عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ؟ فَقَالَ: سَمِعْتُ عَمْرَو بْنَ مَيْمُونٍ يَقُولُ: ﴿يَوْمَ تُبَدَّلُ الأرْضُ غَيْرَ الأرْضِ﴾ قَالَ: أَرْضٌ كَالْفِضَّةِ الْبَيْضَاءِ نَقِيَّةٌ، لَمْ يُسْفَكْ فِيهَا دَمٌ، وَلَمْ يُعْمَلْ عَلَيْهَا خَطِيئَةٌ، يُنْفِذُهُمُ الْبَصَرُ، وَيُسْمِعُهُمُ الدَّاعِي، حُفَاةً عُرَاةً كَمَا خُلِقُوا. قَالَ: أُرَاهُ قَالَ: قِيَامًا حَتَّى يُلجِمَهم الْعَرَقُ .

وَرُوِيَ مِنْ وَجْهٍ آخَرَ عَنْ شُعْبَةَ عَنْ إِسْرَائِيلَ، عَنْ أَبِي إِسْحَاقَ، عَنْ عَمْرِو بْنِ مَيْمُونٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ مَسْعُودٍ، بِنَحْوِهِ. وَكَذَا رَوَاهُ عَاصِمٌ، عَنْ زِرٍّ، عَنِ ابْنِ مَسْعُودٍ، بِهِ.

وَقَالَ سُفْيَانُ الثَّوْرِيُّ، عَنْ أَبِي إِسْحَاقَ، عَنِ عَمْرِو بْنِ مَيْمُونٍ، لَمْ يُخْبِرْ بِهِ. أَوْرَدَ ذَلِكَ كُلَّهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ .

وَقَدْ قَالَ الْحَافِظُ أَبُو بَكْرٍ الْبَزَّارُ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عُبَيد بْنِ عَقِيل، حَدَّثَنَا سَهْلُ بْنُ حَمَّادٍ أَبُو عَتَّابٍ، حَدَّثَنَا جَرِيرُ بْنُ أَيُّوبَ، عَنْ أَبِي إِسْحَاقَ، عَنْ عَمْرِو بْنِ مَيْمُونٍ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ فِي قَوْلِ اللَّهِ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ: ﴿يَوْمَ تُبَدَّلُ الأرْضُ غَيْرَ الأرْضِ﴾ قَالَ: "أَرْضٌ بَيْضَاءُ لَمْ يَسْقُطْ عَلَيْهَا دَمٌ وَلَمْ يُعْمَلْ عَلَيْهَا خَطِيئَةٌ". ثُمَّ قَالَ: لَا نَعْلَمُ رَفَعَهُ إِلَّا جَرِيرُ بْنُ أَيُّوبَ، وَلَيْسَ بِالْقَوِيِّ .

ثُمَّ قَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو كُرَيْبٍ، حدثا مُعَاوِيَةُ بْنُ هِشَامٍ، عَنْ سِنَانٍ عَنْ جَابِرٍ الجُعْفي، عَنْ أَبِي جُبَيرة عَنْ زَيْدٍ قَالَ: أَرْسَلَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ إِلَى الْيَهُودِ فَقَالَ: "هَلْ تَدْرُونَ لِمَ أَرْسَلْتُ إِلَيْهِمْ؟ " قَالُوا: اللَّهُ وَرَسُولُهُ أَعْلَمُ. قَالَ: "أَرْسَلْتُ إِلَيْهِمْ أَسْأَلُهُمْ عَنْ قَوْلِ اللَّهِ: ﴿يَوْمَ تُبَدَّلُ الأرْضُ غَيْرَ الأرْضِ﴾ إِنَّهَا تَكُونُ يَوْمَئِذٍ بَيْضَاءَ مِثْلَ الْفِضَّةِ". فَلَمَّا جَاءُوا سَأَلَهُمْ فَقَالُوا: تَكُونُ بَيْضَاءَ مِثْلَ النَّقِي .

وَهَكَذَا رَوى عَنْ عَلِيٍّ، وَابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، وَأَنَسِ بْنِ مَالِكٍ، وَمُجَاهِدِ بْنِ جبير: أَنَّهَا تُبَدَّلُ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ بِأَرْضٍ مِنْ فِضَّةٍ.

وَعَنْ عَلِيٍّ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، أَنَّهُ قَالَ: تصير الأرض فضة، والسموات ذهبا.

وَقَالَ الرَّبِيعِ: عَنْ أَبِي الْعَالِيَةِ، عَنْ أُبَيِّ بْنِ كَعْبٍ قَالَ: تَصِيرُ السَّمَوَاتُ جِنَانًا.

وَقَالَ أَبُو مِعْشر، عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ كَعْبٍ الْقُرَظِيِّ، أَوْ عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ قَيْسٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿يَوْمَ تُبَدَّلُ الأرْضُ غَيْرَ الأرْضِ﴾ قَالَ: [تُبَدَّلُ] خُبْزَةً يَأْكُلُ مِنْهَا الْمُؤْمِنُونَ مِنْ تَحْتِ أَقْدَامِهِمْ .

وَكَذَا رَوَى وَكِيع، عَنْ عُمَرَ بْنِ بَشِيرٍ الْهَمْدَانِيِّ، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْرٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿يَوْمَ تُبَدَّلُ الأرْضُ غَيْرَ الأرْضِ﴾ قَالَ: تُبَدَّلُ خُبْزَةً بَيْضَاءَ، يَأْكُلُ الْمُؤْمِنُ مِنْ تَحْتِ قَدَمَيْهِ.

وَقَالَ الْأَعْمَشُ، عَنْ خَيْثَمة قَالَ: قَالَ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ -هُوَ ابْنُ مَسْعُودٍ-: الْأَرْضُ كُلُّهَا يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ نَارٌ، وَالْجَنَّةُ مِنْ وَرَائِهَا تَرَى كَوَاعِبَهَا وَأَكْوَابَهَا، ويُلجِمُ النَّاسَ العرقُ، أَوْ يَبْلُغُ مِنْهُمُ الْعَرَقُ، وَلَمْ يَبْلَغُوا الْحِسَابَ.

وَقَالَ الْأَعْمَشُ أَيْضًا، عَنِ المِنْهَال بْنِ عَمْرٍو، عَنْ قَيْسِ بْنِ السَّكَنِ قَالَ: قَالَ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ: الْأَرْضُ كُلُّهَا نَارٌ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ، [وَ] الْجَنَّةُ مِنْ وَرَائِهَا، تَرَى أَكْوَابَهَا وَكَوَاعِبَهَا، وَالَّذِي نَفْسُ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بِيَدِهِ، إِنَّ الرَّجُلَ لَيَفِيضُ عَرَقًا حَتَّى تَرْسَخَ فِي الْأَرْضِ قَدَمُهُ، ثُمَّ يَرْتَفِعُ حَتَّى يَبْلُغَ أَنْفَهُ، وَمَا مَسَّهُ الْحِسَابُ. قَالُوا مِمَّ ذَاكَ يَا أَبَا عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ؟ قَالَ: مِمَّا يَرَى النَّاسَ يَلْقَوْنَ .

وَقَالَ أَبُو جَعْفَرٍ الرَّازِيُّ، عَنِ الرَّبِيعِ بْنِ أَنَسٍ، عَنْ كَعْبٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿يَوْمَ تُبَدَّلُ الأرْضُ غَيْرَ الأرْضِ وَالسَّمَاوَاتُ﴾ قَالَ: تَصِيرُ السَّمَوَاتُ جِنَانًا، وَيَصِيرُ مَكَانُ الْبَحْرِ نَارًا، وَتُبَدَّلُ الْأَرْضُ غَيْرَهَا.

وَفِي الْحَدِيثِ الَّذِي رَوَاهُ أَبُو دَاوُدَ: "لَا يَرْكَبُ الْبَحْرَ إِلَّا غَازٍ أَوْ حَاجٌّ أَوْ مُعْتَمِرٌ، فَإِنَّ تَحْتَ الْبَحْرِ نَارًا -أَوْ: تَحْتَ النَّارِ بَحْرًا". 

وَفِي حَدِيثِ الصُّوَرِ الْمَشْهُورِ الْمَرْوِيِّ عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: "تُبَدَّلُ الْأَرْضُ غَيْرَ الْأَرْضِ وَالسَّمَوَاتُ، فَيَبْسُطُهَا وَيَمُدُّهَا مَدَّ الْأَدِيمِ الْعُكَاظِيِّ، لَا تَرَى فِيهَا عِوَجًا وَلَا أَمْتًا، ثُمَّ يَزْجُرُ اللَّهُ الْخَلْقَ زَجْرَةً، فَإِذَا هُمْ فِي هَذِهِ الْمُبْدَلَةِ" .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَبَرَزُوا لِلَّهِ﴾ أَيْ: خَرَجَتِ الْخَلَائِقُ جَمِيعُهَا مِنْ قُبُورِهِمْ لله ﴿الْوَاحِدِ الْقَهَّارِ﴾ أي: الذي قَهَرَ كُلَّ شَيْءٍ وَغَلَبَهُ، وَدَانَتْ لَهُ الرِّقَابُ، وَخَضَعَتْ لَهُ الْأَلْبَابُ.

---

## 14:49-51 — verses 49-51 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says: {On the Day when the earth will be changed into another earth, and the heavens likewise}, and creation comes forth before its Judge. You will see, O Muhammad, on that Day the criminals, meaning those who committed crime through their disbelief and their corruption, {bound together}, that is, some of them to others, the counterparts or the similar kinds among them having been gathered, each category to its category, just as the Almighty said: {Gather those who did wrong and their counterparts} [al-Saffat: 22], and He said: {And when the souls are paired} [al-Takwir: 7], and He said: {And when they are thrown into it into a narrow place, bound together, they will cry out there for destruction} [al-Furqan: 13], and He said: {And the devils, every builder and diver, and others bound together in chains} [Sad: 37, 38].

The asfad (chains) are fetters, so said Ibn Abbas, Sa'id ibn Jubayr, al-A'mash, and Abd al-Rahman ibn Zayd. This is well known in the language, as Amr ibn Kulthum said:

"So they returned with the garments and with the captives, and we returned with the kings bound in chains."

His saying: {Their garments will be of qatiran} means the clothes which they wear upon themselves will be of qatiran, which is the substance with which camels are smeared, that is, coated, so said Qatadah. It is the substance most apt to stick to fire.

It is pronounced both as "qatiraan" (with fatha on the qaf and kasra on the ta), and with fatha on the qaf and sukun on the ta, and with kasra on the qaf and sukun on the ta. From this comes the saying of Abu al-Najm:

"As if qitran, when it follows it, the wind casts it toward its flowing course."

Ibn Abbas used to say that al-qatran is molten copper, and he sometimes recited it as: "Sarabiluhum min qitran," meaning from copper that is hot, whose heat has reached its utmost. The same has been related from Mujahid, Ikrimah, Sa'id ibn Jubayr, al-Hasan, and Qatadah.

His saying: {And the fire will cover their faces} is like His saying: {The Fire will scorch their faces, and they will be therein with lips distorted} [al-Mu'minun: 104].

Imam Ahmad, may God have mercy on him, said: [chain] Abu Malik al-Ash'ari said: The Messenger of God ﷺ said: "Four things belong to the affair of the Jahiliyyah (pre-Islamic ignorance) and must not be left off: boasting of noble lineage, disparaging people's ancestries, seeking rain by the stars, and wailing over the dead. And the wailing woman, if she does not repent before her death, will be made to stand on the Day of Resurrection wearing a garment of qatiran and a shirt of scabies (jarab)." Muslim alone transmitted it.

And in the hadith of al-Qasim, from Abu Umamah, may God be pleased with him, he said: The Messenger of God ﷺ said: "The wailing woman, if she does not repent, will be made to stand in a path between Paradise and the Fire, her garments will be of qatiran, and the Fire will cover her face."

His saying: {So that God may recompense} means on the Day of Resurrection, just as He said: {So that He may recompense those who did evil for what they did, and recompense those who did good with the best reward} [al-Najm: 31].

{Indeed, God is swift in reckoning}: it is possible that this is like His saying: {The reckoning has drawn near for mankind, while they are in heedlessness, turning away}. And it is possible that it means that in the state of His reckoning with His servant, He is swift in bringing it to completion, because He knows all things and nothing hidden is concealed from Him, and all of creation, in relation to His power, is like a single one of them, as in His saying: {Your creation and your resurrection are not but like that of a single soul} [Luqman: 28]. This is the meaning of Mujahid's saying: {swift in reckoning} means swift in enumeration.

It is also possible that both meanings are intended together, and God knows best.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: ﴿يَوْمَ تُبَدَّلُ الأرْضُ غَيْرَ الأرْضِ وَالسَّمَاوَاتُ﴾ وَتَبْرُزُ الْخَلَائِقُ لديَّانها، تَرَى يَا مُحَمَّدُ يَوْمَئِذٍ الْمُجْرِمِينَ، وَهُمُ الَّذِينَ أَجْرَمُوا بِكُفْرِهِمْ وَفَسَادِهِمْ، ﴿مُقَرَّنِينَ﴾ أَيْ: بَعْضُهُمْ إِلَى بَعْضٍ، قَدْ جُمِعَ بَيْنَ النُّظَرَاءِ أَوِ الْأَشْكَالِ مِنْهُمْ، كُلِّ صِنْفٍ إِلَى صِنْفٍ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿احْشُرُوا الَّذِينَ ظَلَمُوا وَأَزْوَاجَهُمْ﴾ [الصَّافَّاتِ: ٢٢] ، وَقَالَ: ﴿وَإِذَا النُّفُوسُ زُوِّجَتْ﴾ [التَّكْوِيرِ: ٧] ، وَقَالَ: ﴿وَإِذَا أُلْقُوا مِنْهَا مَكَانًا ضَيِّقًا مُقَرَّنِينَ دَعَوْا هُنَالِكَ ثُبُورًا﴾ [الْفُرْقَانِ: ١٣] ، وَقَالَ: ﴿وَالشَّيَاطِينَ كُلَّ بَنَّاءٍ وَغَوَّاصٍ وَآخَرِينَ مُقَرَّنِينَ فِي الأصْفَادِ﴾ [ص: ٣٧، ٣٨] .

وَالْأَصْفَادُ: هِيَ الْقُيُودُ، قَالَهُ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ، وَسَعِيدُ بْنُ جُبَيْرٍ، وَالْأَعْمَشُ، وَعَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ زَيْدٍ. وَهُوَ مَشْهُورٌ فِي اللُّغَةِ، قَالَ عَمْرُو بْنُ كُلْثُومٍ.

فَآبُوا بِالثِّيَابِ وَبِالسَّبَايَا وأُبْنَا بالمُلُوك مُصَفّدينا 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿سَرَابِيلُهُمْ مِنْ قَطِرَانٍ﴾ أَيْ: ثِيَابُهُمُ الَّتِي يَلْبَسُونَهَا عَلَيْهِمْ مِنْ قَطِرَانٍ، وَهُوَ الَّذِي تُهنأ بِهِ الْإِبِلُ، أَيْ: تُطْلَى، قَالَهُ قَتَادَةُ. وَهُوَ أَلْصَقُ شَيْءٍ بِالنَّارِ.

وَيُقَالُ فِيهِ: "قَطِران"، بِفَتْحِ الْقَافِ وَكَسْرِ الطَّاءِ، وَبِفَتْحِ الْقَافِ وَتَسْكِينِ الطَّاءِ، وَبِكَسْرِ الْقَافِ وَتَسْكِينِ الطَّاءِ، وَمِنْهُ قَوْلُ أَبِي النَّجْمِ.

كَأَنَّ قِطْرانًا إذَا تَلاهَا ... تَرْمي بِهِ الرِّيحُ إِلَى مَجْراها 

وَكَانَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ يَقُولُ: القَطران هُوَ: النُّحَاسُ الْمُذَابُ، وَرُبَّمَا قَرَأَهَا: "سَرَابيلهم مِنْ قَطِران" أَيْ: مِنْ نُحَاسٍ حَارٍّ قَدِ انْتَهَى حَرُّهُ. وَكَذَا رُوِيَ عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ، وَعِكْرِمَةَ، وَسَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَير، وَالْحَسَنِ، وَقَتَادَةَ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَتَغْشَى وُجُوهَهُمُ النَّارُ﴾ كَقَوْلِهِ: ﴿تَلْفَحُ وُجُوهَهُمُ النَّارُ وَهُمْ فِيهَا كَالِحُونَ﴾ [الْمُؤْمِنُونَ: ١٠٤] .

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ: حَدَّثَنَا يَحْيَى بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ، أَنْبَأَنَا أَبَانُ بْنُ يَزِيدَ، عن يحيى بن أبي كَثِيرٍ، عَنْ زَيْدٍ، عَنْ أَبِي سَلَّامٍ، عَنْ أَبِي مَالِكٍ الْأَشْعَرِيِّ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "أَرْبَعٌ مِنْ أَمْرِ الْجَاهِلِيَّةِ لَا يُتْرَكن الْفَخْرُ بِالْأَحْسَابِ، وَالطَّعْنُ فِي الْأَنْسَابِ، وَالِاسْتِسْقَاءُ بِالنُّجُومِ، وَالنِّيَاحَةُ، وَالنَّائِحَةُ إِذَا لَمْ تَتُبْ قَبْلَ مَوْتِهَا، تُقَامُ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ وَعَلَيْهَا سِرْبَالٌ مِنْ قَطِرَانٍ، ودرْع مِنْ جَرَب". انْفَرَدَ بِإِخْرَاجِهِ مُسْلِمٌ .

وَفِي حَدِيثِ الْقَاسِمِ، عَنْ أَبِي أُمَامَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "النَّائِحَةُ إِذَا لَمْ تَتُبْ، تُوقَفُ فِي طَرِيقٍ بَيْنَ الْجَنَّةِ وَالنَّارِ، وَسَرَابِيلُهَا مِنْ قَطِرَانٍ، وَتَغْشَى وَجْهَهَا النَّارُ" .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿لِيَجْزِيَ اللَّهُ﴾ أَيْ: يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ، كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿لِيَجْزِيَ الَّذِينَ أَسَاءُوا بِمَا عَمِلُوا وَيَجْزِيَ الَّذِينَ أَحْسَنُوا بِالْحُسْنَى﴾ [النَّجْمِ: ٣١] .

﴿إِنَّ اللَّهَ سَرِيعُ الْحِسَابِ﴾ يُحْتَمَلُ أَنْ يَكُونَ كَقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿اقْتَرَبَ لِلنَّاسِ حِسَابُهُمْ وَهُمْ فِي غَفْلَةٍ مُعْرِضُونَ﴾ وَيُحْتَمَلُ أَنَّهُ فِي حَالِ مُحَاسَبَتِهِ لِعَبْدِهِ سَرِيعُ النَّجاز؛ لِأَنَّهُ يَعْلَمُ كُلَّ شَيْءٍ، وَلَا يَخْفَى عَلَيْهِ خَافِيَةٌ، وَإِنَّ جَمِيعَ الْخَلْقِ بِالنِّسْبَةِ إِلَى قُدْرَتِهِ كَالْوَاحِدِ مِنْهُمْ، كَقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿مَا خَلْقُكُمْ وَلا بَعْثُكُمْ إِلا كَنَفْسٍ وَاحِدَةٍ﴾ [لُقْمَانَ: ٢٨] ، وَهَذَا مَعْنَى قَوْلِ مُجَاهِدٍ: ﴿سَرِيعُ الْحِسَابِ﴾ [إِحْصَاءً] .

وَيُحْتَمَلُ أَنْ يَكُونَ الْمَعْنَيَانِ مُرَادَيْنِ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

---

## 14:52 — verse 52

### Translation

He, Exalted, says: this Qur'an is a message conveyed to mankind, as in His saying: {that I may warn you thereby, and whomever it reaches} [al-An'am: 19], meaning it is a message conveyed to all of creation, both jinn and mankind, just as He said at the beginning of the surah: {Alif, Lam, Ra. A Book which We have sent down to you that you may bring mankind out of the darknesses into the light, by permission of their Lord}.

{And that they may be warned thereby}, meaning that they may take admonition by it, {and that they may know that He is but One God}, meaning that they draw evidence from what it contains of proofs and indications that there is no god but Him, {and that those possessed of understanding may take heed}, meaning those possessed of intellects.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: هَذَا الْقُرْآنُ بَلَاغٌ لِلنَّاسِ، كَقَوْلِهِ: ﴿لأنْذِرَكُمْ بِهِ وَمَنْ بَلَغَ﴾ [الْأَنْعَامِ: ١٩] ، أَيْ: هُوَ بَلَاغٌ لِجَمِيعِ الْخَلْقِ مِنْ إِنْسٍ وَجَانٍّ، كَمَا قَالَ فِي أَوَّلِ السُّورَةِ: ﴿الر كِتَابٌ أَنزلْنَاهُ إِلَيْكَ لِتُخْرِجَ النَّاسَ مِنَ الظُّلُمَاتِ إِلَى النُّورِ بِإِذْنِ رَبِّهِمْ﴾

﴿وَلِيُنْذَرُوا بِهِ﴾ أَيْ: لِيَتَّعِظُوا بِهِ، ﴿وَلِيَعْلَمُوا أَنَّمَا هُوَ إِلَهٌ وَاحِدٌ﴾ أَيْ: يَسْتَدِلُّوا بِمَا فِيهِ مِنَ الْحُجَجِ وَالدَّلَالَاتِ عَلَى أَنَّهُ لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا هُوَ ﴿وَلِيَذَّكَّرَ أُولُو الألْبَابِ﴾ أَيْ: ذَوُو الْعُقُولِ.

---
